\PsalmChap{25}{\D By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}To you, Yahweh, I lift up my soul.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}My God, I have trusted in you.
\par }{\QB Don’t let me be shamed.
\par }{\QB Don’t let my enemies triumph over me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Yes, no one who waits for you will be shamed.
\par }{\QB They will be shamed who deal treacherously without cause.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{4}Show me your ways, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB Teach me your paths.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Guide me in your truth, and teach me,
\par }{\QB For you are the God of my salvation,
\par }{\QB I wait for you all day long.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Yahweh, remember your tender mercies and your loving kindness,
\par }{\QB for they are from old times.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Don’t remember the sins of my youth, nor my transgressions.
\par }{\QB Remember me according to your loving kindness,
\par }{\QB for your goodness’ sake, Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Good and upright is Yahweh,
\par }{\QB therefore he will instruct sinners in the way.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}He will guide the humble in justice.
\par }{\QB He will teach the humble his way.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}All the paths of Yahweh are loving kindness and truth
\par }{\QB to such as keep his covenant and his testimonies.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}For your name’s sake, Yahweh,
\par }{\QB pardon my iniquity, for it is great.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}What man is he who fears Yahweh?
\par }{\QB He shall instruct him in the way that he shall choose.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}His soul will dwell at ease.
\par }{\QB His offspring will inherit the land.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}The friendship of Yahweh is with those who fear him.
\par }{\QB He will show them his covenant.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{15}My eyes are ever on Yahweh,
\par }{\QB for he will pluck my feet out of the net.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Turn to me, and have mercy on me,
\par }{\QB for I am desolate and afflicted.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}The troubles of my heart are enlarged.
\par }{\QB Oh bring me out of my distresses.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Consider my affliction and my travail.
\par }{\QB Forgive all my sins.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Consider my enemies, for they are many.
\par }{\QB They hate me with cruel hatred.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Oh keep my soul, and deliver me.
\par }{\QB Let me not be disappointed, for I take refuge in you.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Let integrity and uprightness preserve me,
\par }{\QB for I wait for you.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}Redeem Israel, God,
\par }{\QB out of all his troubles.

\par }\PsalmChap{26}{\D By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Judge me, Yahweh, for I have walked in my integrity.
\par }{\QB I have trusted also in Yahweh without wavering.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Examine me, Yahweh, and prove me.
\par }{\QB Try my heart and my mind.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For your loving kindness is before my eyes.
\par }{\QB I have walked in your truth.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}I have not sat with deceitful men,
\par }{\QB neither will I go in with hypocrites.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}I hate the assembly of evildoers,
\par }{\QB and will not sit with the wicked.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I will wash my hands in innocence,
\par }{\QB so I will go about your altar, Yahweh,
\par }{\QB \VS{7}that I may make the voice of thanksgiving to be heard
\par }{\QB and tell of all your wondrous deeds.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Yahweh, I love the habitation of your house,
\par }{\QB the place where your glory dwells.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Don’t gather my soul with sinners,
\par }{\QB nor my life with bloodthirsty men;
\par }{\QB \VS{10}in whose hands is wickedness,
\par }{\QB their right hand is full of bribes.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{11}But as for me, I will walk in my integrity.
\par }{\QB Redeem me, and be merciful to me.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}My foot stands in an even place.
\par }{\QB In the congregations I will bless Yahweh.

\par }\PsalmChap{27}{\D By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Yahweh is my light and my salvation.
\par }{\QB Whom shall I fear?
\par }{\Q Yahweh is the strength of my life.
\par }{\QB Of whom shall I be afraid?
\par }{\Q \VS{2}When evildoers came at me to eat up my flesh,
\par }{\QB even my adversaries and my foes, they stumbled and fell.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Though an army should encamp against me,
\par }{\QB my heart shall not fear.
\par }{\Q Though war should rise against me,
\par }{\QB even then I will be confident.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}One thing I have asked of Yahweh, that I will seek after:
\par }{\QB that I may dwell in Yahweh’s house all the days of my life,
\par }{\QB to see Yahweh’s beauty,
\par }{\QB and to inquire in his temple.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}For in the day of trouble, he will keep me secretly in his pavilion.
\par }{\QB In the secret place of his tabernacle, he will hide me.
\par }{\QB He will lift me up on a rock.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Now my head will be lifted up above my enemies around me.
\par }{\Q I will offer sacrifices of joy in his tent.
\par }{\QB I will sing, yes, I will sing praises to Yahweh.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{7}Hear, Yahweh, when I cry with my voice.
\par }{\QB Have mercy also on me, and answer me.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}When you said, “Seek my face,”
\par }{\QB my heart said to you, “I will seek your face, Yahweh.”
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Don’t hide your face from me.
\par }{\QB Don’t put your servant away in anger.
\par }{\Q You have been my help.
\par }{\QB Don’t abandon me,
\par }{\QB neither forsake me, God of my salvation.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}When my father and my mother forsake me,
\par }{\QB then Yahweh will take me up.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Teach me your way, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB Lead me in a straight path, because of my enemies.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Don’t deliver me over to the desire of my adversaries,
\par }{\QB for false witnesses have risen up against me,
\par }{\QB such as breathe out cruelty.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}I am still confident of this:
\par }{\QB I will see the goodness of Yahweh in the land of the living.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Wait for Yahweh.
\par }{\QB Be strong, and let your heart take courage.
\par }{\Q Yes, wait for Yahweh.

\par }\PsalmChap{28}{\D By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}To you, Yahweh, I call.
\par }{\QB My rock, don’t be deaf to me,
\par }{\QB lest, if you are silent to me,
\par }{\QB I would become like those who go down into the pit.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Hear the voice of my petitions, when I cry to you,
\par }{\QB when I lift up my hands toward your Most Holy Place.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Don’t draw me away with the wicked,
\par }{\QB with the workers of iniquity who speak peace with their neighbors,
\par }{\QB but mischief is in their hearts.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Give them according to their work, and according to the wickedness of their doings.
\par }{\QB Give them according to the operation of their hands.
\par }{\QB Bring back on them what they deserve.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Because they don’t respect the works of Yahweh,
\par }{\QB nor the operation of his hands,
\par }{\QB he will break them down and not build them up.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{6}Blessed be Yahweh,
\par }{\QB because he has heard the voice of my petitions.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Yahweh is my strength and my shield.
\par }{\QB My heart has trusted in him, and I am helped.
\par }{\Q Therefore my heart greatly rejoices.
\par }{\QB With my song I will thank him.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Yahweh is their strength.
\par }{\QB He is a stronghold of salvation to his anointed.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Save your people,
\par }{\QB and bless your inheritance.
\par }{\Q Be their shepherd also,
\par }{\QB and bear them up forever.

\par }\PsalmChap{29}{\D A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Ascribe to Yahweh, you sons of the mighty,
\par }{\QB ascribe to Yahweh glory and strength.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Ascribe to Yahweh the glory due to his name.
\par }{\QB Worship Yahweh in holy array.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{3}Yahweh’s voice is on the waters.
\par }{\QB The God of glory thunders, even Yahweh on many waters.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Yahweh’s voice is powerful.
\par }{\QB Yahweh’s voice is full of majesty.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Yahweh’s voice breaks the cedars.
\par }{\QB Yes, Yahweh breaks in pieces the cedars of Lebanon.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}He makes them also to skip like a calf;
\par }{\QB Lebanon and Sirion like a young, wild ox.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Yahweh’s voice strikes with flashes of lightning.
\par }{\QB \VS{8}Yahweh’s voice shakes the wilderness.
\par }{\QB Yahweh shakes the wilderness of Kadesh.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Yahweh’s voice makes the deer calve,
\par }{\QB and strips the forests bare.
\par }{\QB In his temple everything says, “Glory!”
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{10}Yahweh sat enthroned at the Flood.
\par }{\QB Yes, Yahweh sits as King forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Yahweh will give strength to his people.
\par }{\QB Yahweh will bless his people with peace.

\par }\PsalmChap{30}{\D A Psalm. A Song for the Dedication of the Temple. By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}I will extol you, Yahweh, for you have raised me up,
\par }{\QB and have not made my foes to rejoice over me.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Yahweh my God, I cried to you,
\par }{\QB and you have healed me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Yahweh, you have brought up my soul from Sheol.\FTNT{*}{{\FR 30:3 }
Sheol is the place of the dead.}
\par }{\QB You have kept me alive, that I should not go down to the pit.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Sing praise to Yahweh, you saints of his.
\par }{\QB Give thanks to his holy name.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}For his anger is but for a moment.
\par }{\QB His favor is for a lifetime.
\par }{\Q Weeping may stay for the night,
\par }{\QB but joy comes in the morning.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}As for me, I said in my prosperity,
\par }{\QB “I shall never be moved.”
\par }{\Q \VS{7}You, Yahweh, when you favored me, made my mountain stand strong;
\par }{\QB but when you hid your face, I was troubled.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}I cried to you, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB I made supplication to the Lord:
\par }{\Q \VS{9}“What profit is there in my destruction, if I go down to the pit?
\par }{\QB Shall the dust praise you?
\par }{\QB Shall it declare your truth?
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Hear, Yahweh, and have mercy on me.
\par }{\QB Yahweh, be my helper.”
\par }{\Q \VS{11}You have turned my mourning into dancing for me.
\par }{\QB You have removed my sackcloth, and clothed me with gladness,
\par }{\QB \VS{12}to the end that my heart may sing praise to you, and not be silent.
\par }{\Q Yahweh my God, I will give thanks to you forever!

\par }\PsalmChap{31}{\D For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}In you, Yahweh, I take refuge.
\par }{\QB Let me never be disappointed.
\par }{\QB Deliver me in your righteousness.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Bow down your ear to me.
\par }{\QB Deliver me speedily.
\par }{\Q Be to me a strong rock,
\par }{\QB a house of defense to save me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For you are my rock and my fortress,
\par }{\QB therefore for your name’s sake lead me and guide me.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Pluck me out of the net that they have laid secretly for me,
\par }{\QB for you are my stronghold.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Into your hand I commend my spirit.
\par }{\QB You redeem me, Yahweh, God of truth.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I hate those who regard lying vanities,
\par }{\QB but I trust in Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}I will be glad and rejoice in your loving kindness,
\par }{\QB for you have seen my affliction.
\par }{\QB You have known my soul in adversities.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}You have not shut me up into the hand of the enemy.
\par }{\QB You have set my feet in a large place.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Have mercy on me, Yahweh, for I am in distress.
\par }{\QB My eye, my soul, and my body waste away with grief.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}For my life is spent with sorrow,
\par }{\QB my years with sighing.
\par }{\Q My strength fails because of my iniquity.
\par }{\QB My bones are wasted away.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Because of all my adversaries I have become utterly contemptible to my neighbors,
\par }{\QB a horror to my acquaintances.
\par }{\QB Those who saw me on the street fled from me.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}I am forgotten from their hearts like a dead man.
\par }{\QB I am like broken pottery.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}For I have heard the slander of many, terror on every side,
\par }{\QB while they conspire together against me,
\par }{\QB they plot to take away my life.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}But I trust in you, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB I said, “You are my God.”
\par }{\Q \VS{15}My times are in your hand.
\par }{\QB Deliver me from the hand of my enemies, and from those who persecute me.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Make your face to shine on your servant.
\par }{\QB Save me in your loving kindness.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Let me not be disappointed, Yahweh, for I have called on you.
\par }{\QB Let the wicked be disappointed.
\par }{\QB Let them be silent in Sheol.\FTNT{*}{{\FR 31:17 }
Sheol is the place of the dead.}
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Let the lying lips be mute,
\par }{\QB which speak against the righteous insolently, with pride and contempt.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Oh how great is your goodness,
\par }{\QB which you have laid up for those who fear you,
\par }{\QB which you have worked for those who take refuge in you,
\par }{\QB before the sons of men!
\par }{\Q \VS{20}In the shelter of your presence you will hide them from the plotting of man.
\par }{\QB You will keep them secretly in a dwelling away from the strife of tongues.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Praise be to Yahweh,
\par }{\QB for he has shown me his marvelous loving kindness in a strong city.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}As for me, I said in my haste, “I am cut off from before your eyes.”
\par }{\QB Nevertheless you heard the voice of my petitions when I cried to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Oh love Yahweh, all you his saints!
\par }{\QB Yahweh preserves the faithful,
\par }{\Q and fully recompenses him who behaves arrogantly.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}Be strong, and let your heart take courage,
\par }{\QB all you who hope in Yahweh.

\par }\PsalmChap{32}{\D By David. A contemplative psalm.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Blessed is he whose disobedience is forgiven,
\par }{\QB whose sin is covered.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Blessed is the man to whom Yahweh doesn’t impute iniquity,
\par }{\QB in whose spirit there is no deceit.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}When I kept silence, my bones wasted away through my groaning all day long.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For day and night your hand was heavy on me.
\par }{\QB My strength was sapped in the heat of summer.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{5}I acknowledged my sin to you.
\par }{\QB I didn’t hide my iniquity.
\par }{\Q I said, I will confess my transgressions to Yahweh,
\par }{\QB and you forgave the iniquity of my sin.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{6}For this, let everyone who is godly pray to you in a time when you may be found.
\par }{\QB Surely when the great waters overflow, they shall not reach to him.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}You are my hiding place.
\par }{\QB You will preserve me from trouble.
\par }{\QB You will surround me with songs of deliverance.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{8}I will instruct you and teach you in the way which you shall go.
\par }{\QB I will counsel you with my eye on you.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Don’t be like the horse, or like the mule, which have no understanding,
\par }{\QB who are controlled by bit and bridle, or else they will not come near to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Many sorrows come to the wicked,
\par }{\QB but loving kindness shall surround him who trusts in Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Be glad in Yahweh, and rejoice, you righteous!
\par }{\QB Shout for joy, all you who are upright in heart!

\par }\PsalmChap{33}{\Q \VerseOne{1}Rejoice in Yahweh, you righteous!
\par }{\QB Praise is fitting for the upright.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Give thanks to Yahweh with the lyre.
\par }{\QB Sing praises to him with the harp of ten strings.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Sing to him a new song.
\par }{\QB Play skillfully with a shout of joy!
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For Yahweh’s word is right.
\par }{\QB All his work is done in faithfulness.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}He loves righteousness and justice.
\par }{\QB The earth is full of the loving kindness of Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}By Yahweh’s word, the heavens were made:
\par }{\QB all their army by the breath of his mouth.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}He gathers the waters of the sea together as a heap.
\par }{\QB He lays up the deeps in storehouses.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Let all the earth fear Yahweh.
\par }{\QB Let all the inhabitants of the world stand in awe of him.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}For he spoke, and it was done.
\par }{\QB He commanded, and it stood firm.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Yahweh brings the counsel of the nations to nothing.
\par }{\QB He makes the thoughts of the peoples to be of no effect.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}The counsel of Yahweh stands fast forever,
\par }{\QB the thoughts of his heart to all generations.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Blessed is the nation whose God is Yahweh,
\par }{\QB the people whom he has chosen for his own inheritance.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Yahweh looks from heaven.
\par }{\QB He sees all the sons of men.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}From the place of his habitation he looks out on all the inhabitants of the earth,
\par }{\QB \VS{15}he who fashions all of their hearts;
\par }{\QB and he considers all of their works.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}There is no king saved by the multitude of an army.
\par }{\QB A mighty man is not delivered by great strength.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}A horse is a vain thing for safety,
\par }{\QB neither does he deliver any by his great power.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Behold, Yahweh’s eye is on those who fear him,
\par }{\QB on those who hope in his loving kindness,
\par }{\QB \VS{19}to deliver their soul from death,
\par }{\QB to keep them alive in famine.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Our soul has waited for Yahweh.
\par }{\QB He is our help and our shield.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}For our heart rejoices in him,
\par }{\QB because we have trusted in his holy name.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}Let your loving kindness be on us, Yahweh,
\par }{\QB since we have hoped in you.

\par }\PsalmChap{34}{\D By David; when he pretended to be insane before Abimelech, who drove him away, and he departed.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}\FTNT{*}{{\FR 34:1 }
Psalm 34 is an acrostic poem, with each verse starting with a letter of the alphabet (ordered from Alef to Tav).} I will bless Yahweh at all times.
\par }{\QB His praise will always be in my mouth.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}My soul shall boast in Yahweh.
\par }{\QB The humble shall hear of it and be glad.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Oh magnify Yahweh with me.
\par }{\QB Let’s exalt his name together.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}I sought Yahweh, and he answered me,
\par }{\QB and delivered me from all my fears.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They looked to him, and were radiant.
\par }{\QB Their faces shall never be covered with shame.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}This poor man cried, and Yahweh heard him,
\par }{\QB and saved him out of all his troubles.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Yahweh’s angel encamps around those who fear him,
\par }{\QB and delivers them.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Oh taste and see that Yahweh is good.
\par }{\QB Blessed is the man who takes refuge in him.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Oh fear Yahweh, you his saints,
\par }{\QB for there is no lack with those who fear him.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}The young lions do lack, and suffer hunger,
\par }{\QB but those who seek Yahweh shall not lack any good thing.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{11}Come, you children, listen to me.
\par }{\QB I will teach you the fear of Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Who is someone who desires life,
\par }{\QB and loves many days, that he may see good?
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Keep your tongue from evil,
\par }{\QB and your lips from speaking lies.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Depart from evil, and do good.
\par }{\QB Seek peace, and pursue it.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Yahweh’s eyes are toward the righteous.
\par }{\QB His ears listen to their cry.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Yahweh’s face is against those who do evil,
\par }{\QB to cut off their memory from the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}The righteous cry, and Yahweh hears,
\par }{\QB and delivers them out of all their troubles.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Yahweh is near to those who have a broken heart,
\par }{\QB and saves those who have a crushed spirit.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Many are the afflictions of the righteous,
\par }{\QB but Yahweh delivers him out of them all.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}He protects all of his bones.
\par }{\QB Not one of them is broken.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Evil shall kill the wicked.
\par }{\QB Those who hate the righteous shall be condemned.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}Yahweh redeems the soul of his servants.
\par }{\QB None of those who take refuge in him shall be condemned.

\par }\PsalmChap{35}{\D By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Contend, Yahweh, with those who contend with me.
\par }{\QB Fight against those who fight against me.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Take hold of shield and buckler,
\par }{\QB and stand up for my help.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Brandish the spear and block those who pursue me.
\par }{\QB Tell my soul, “I am your salvation.”
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Let those who seek after my soul be disappointed and brought to dishonor.
\par }{\QB Let those who plot my ruin be turned back and confounded.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Let them be as chaff before the wind,
\par }{\QB Yahweh’s angel driving them on.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Let their way be dark and slippery,
\par }{\QB Yahweh’s angel pursuing them.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}For without cause they have hidden their net in a pit for me.
\par }{\QB Without cause they have dug a pit for my soul.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Let destruction come on him unawares.
\par }{\QB Let his net that he has hidden catch himself.
\par }{\QB Let him fall into that destruction.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{9}My soul shall be joyful in Yahweh.
\par }{\QB It shall rejoice in his salvation.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}All my bones shall say, “Yahweh, who is like you,
\par }{\QB who delivers the poor from him who is too strong for him;
\par }{\QB yes, the poor and the needy from him who robs him?”
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Unrighteous witnesses rise up.
\par }{\QB They ask me about things that I don’t know about.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}They reward me evil for good,
\par }{\QB to the bereaving of my soul.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{13}But as for me, when they were sick, my clothing was sackcloth.
\par }{\QB I afflicted my soul with fasting.
\par }{\QB My prayer returned into my own bosom.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}I behaved myself as though it had been my friend or my brother.
\par }{\QB I bowed down mourning, as one who mourns his mother.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}But in my adversity, they rejoiced, and gathered themselves together.
\par }{\QB The attackers gathered themselves together against me, and I didn’t know it.
\par }{\QB They tore at me, and didn’t cease.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Like the profane mockers in feasts,
\par }{\QB they gnashed their teeth at me.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Lord, how long will you look on?
\par }{\QB Rescue my soul from their destruction,
\par }{\QB my precious life from the lions.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}I will give you thanks in the great assembly.
\par }{\QB I will praise you among many people.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Don’t let those who are my enemies wrongfully rejoice over me;
\par }{\QB neither let those who hate me without a cause wink their eyes.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}For they don’t speak peace,
\par }{\QB but they devise deceitful words against those who are quiet in the land.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Yes, they opened their mouth wide against me.
\par }{\QB They said, “Aha! Aha! Our eye has seen it!”
\par }{\Q \VS{22}You have seen it, Yahweh. Don’t keep silent.
\par }{\QB Lord, don’t be far from me.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Wake up! Rise up to defend me, my God!
\par }{\QB My Lord, contend for me!
\par }{\Q \VS{24}Vindicate me, Yahweh my God, according to your righteousness.
\par }{\QB Don’t let them gloat over me.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}Don’t let them say in their heart, “Aha! That’s the way we want it!”
\par }{\QB Don’t let them say, “We have swallowed him up!”
\par }{\Q \VS{26}Let them be disappointed and confounded together who rejoice at my calamity.
\par }{\QB Let them be clothed with shame and dishonor who magnify themselves against me.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{27}Let those who favor my righteous cause shout for joy and be glad.
\par }{\QB Yes, let them say continually, “May Yahweh be magnified,
\par }{\QB who has pleasure in the prosperity of his servant!”
\par }{\Q \VS{28}My tongue shall talk about your righteousness and about your praise all day long.

\par }\PsalmChap{36}{\D For the Chief Musician. By David, the servant of Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}A revelation is within my heart about the disobedience of the wicked:
\par }{\QB “There is no fear of God before his eyes.”
\par }{\Q \VS{2}For he flatters himself in his own eyes,
\par }{\QB too much to detect and hate his sin.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}The words of his mouth are iniquity and deceit.
\par }{\QB He has ceased to be wise and to do good.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}He plots iniquity on his bed.
\par }{\QB He sets himself in a way that is not good.
\par }{\QB He doesn’t abhor evil.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{5}Your loving kindness, Yahweh, is in the heavens.
\par }{\QB Your faithfulness reaches to the skies.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Your righteousness is like the mountains of God.
\par }{\QB Your judgments are like a great deep.
\par }{\QB Yahweh, you preserve man and animal.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}How precious is your loving kindness, God!
\par }{\QB The children of men take refuge under the shadow of your wings.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}They shall be abundantly satisfied with the abundance of your house.
\par }{\QB You will make them drink of the river of your pleasures.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}For with you is the spring of life.
\par }{\QB In your light we will see light.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Oh continue your loving kindness to those who know you,
\par }{\QB your righteousness to the upright in heart.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Don’t let the foot of pride come against me.
\par }{\QB Don’t let the hand of the wicked drive me away.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}There the workers of iniquity are fallen.
\par }{\QB They are thrust down, and shall not be able to rise.

\par }\PsalmChap{37}{\D By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Don’t fret because of evildoers,
\par }{\QB neither be envious against those who work unrighteousness.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}For they shall soon be cut down like the grass,
\par }{\QB and wither like the green herb.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Trust in Yahweh, and do good.
\par }{\QB Dwell in the land, and enjoy safe pasture.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Also delight yourself in Yahweh,
\par }{\QB and he will give you the desires of your heart.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Commit your way to Yahweh.
\par }{\QB Trust also in him, and he will do this:
\par }{\Q \VS{6}he will make your righteousness shine out like light,
\par }{\QB and your justice as the noon day sun.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Rest in Yahweh, and wait patiently for him.
\par }{\QB Don’t fret because of him who prospers in his way,
\par }{\QB because of the man who makes wicked plots happen.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Cease from anger, and forsake wrath.
\par }{\QB Don’t fret; it leads only to evildoing.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}For evildoers shall be cut off,
\par }{\QB but those who wait for Yahweh shall inherit the land.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}For yet a little while, and the wicked will be no more.
\par }{\QB Yes, though you look for his place, he isn’t there.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}But the humble shall inherit the land,
\par }{\QB and shall delight themselves in the abundance of peace.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}The wicked plots against the just,
\par }{\QB and gnashes at him with his teeth.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}The Lord will laugh at him,
\par }{\QB for he sees that his day is coming.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}The wicked have drawn out the sword, and have bent their bow,
\par }{\QB to cast down the poor and needy,
\par }{\QB to kill those who are upright on the path.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Their sword shall enter into their own heart.
\par }{\QB Their bows shall be broken.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Better is a little that the righteous has,
\par }{\QB than the abundance of many wicked.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}For the arms of the wicked shall be broken,
\par }{\QB but Yahweh upholds the righteous.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Yahweh knows the days of the perfect.
\par }{\QB Their inheritance shall be forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}They shall not be disappointed in the time of evil.
\par }{\QB In the days of famine they shall be satisfied.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{20}But the wicked shall perish.
\par }{\QB The enemies of Yahweh shall be like the beauty of the fields.
\par }{\QB They will vanish—
\par }{\QB vanish like smoke.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}The wicked borrow, and don’t pay back,
\par }{\QB but the righteous give generously.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}For such as are blessed by him shall inherit the land.
\par }{\QB Those who are cursed by him shall be cut off.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}A man’s steps are established by Yahweh.
\par }{\QB He delights in his way.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}Though he stumble, he shall not fall,
\par }{\QB for Yahweh holds him up with his hand.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}I have been young, and now am old,
\par }{\QB yet I have not seen the righteous forsaken,
\par }{\QB nor his children begging for bread.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}All day long he deals graciously, and lends.
\par }{\QB His offspring is blessed.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}Depart from evil, and do good.
\par }{\QB Live securely forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}For Yahweh loves justice,
\par }{\QB and doesn’t forsake his saints.
\par }{\QB They are preserved forever,
\par }{\QB but the children of the wicked shall be cut off.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}The righteous shall inherit the land,
\par }{\QB and live in it forever.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{30}The mouth of the righteous talks of wisdom.
\par }{\QB His tongue speaks justice.
\par }{\Q \VS{31}The law of his God is in his heart.
\par }{\QB None of his steps shall slide.
\par }{\Q \VS{32}The wicked watch the righteous,
\par }{\QB and seek to kill him.
\par }{\Q \VS{33}Yahweh will not leave him in his hand,
\par }{\QB nor condemn him when he is judged.
\par }{\Q \VS{34}Wait for Yahweh, and keep his way,
\par }{\QB and he will exalt you to inherit the land.
\par }{\QB When the wicked are cut off, you shall see it.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{35}I have seen the wicked in great power,
\par }{\QB spreading himself like a green tree in its native soil.
\par }{\Q \VS{36}But he passed away, and behold, he was not.
\par }{\QB Yes, I sought him, but he could not be found.
\par }{\Q \VS{37}Mark the perfect man, and see the upright,
\par }{\QB for there is a future for the man of peace.
\par }{\Q \VS{38}As for transgressors, they shall be destroyed together.
\par }{\QB The future of the wicked shall be cut off.
\par }{\Q \VS{39}But the salvation of the righteous is from Yahweh.
\par }{\QB He is their stronghold in the time of trouble.
\par }{\Q \VS{40}Yahweh helps them and rescues them.
\par }{\QB He rescues them from the wicked and saves them,
\par }{\QB because they have taken refuge in him.

\par }\PsalmChap{38}{\D A Psalm by David, for a memorial.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Yahweh, don’t rebuke me in your wrath,
\par }{\QB neither chasten me in your hot displeasure.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}For your arrows have pierced me,
\par }{\QB your hand presses hard on me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}There is no soundness in my flesh because of your indignation,
\par }{\QB neither is there any health in my bones because of my sin.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For my iniquities have gone over my head.
\par }{\QB As a heavy burden, they are too heavy for me.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}My wounds are loathsome and corrupt
\par }{\QB because of my foolishness.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I am in pain and bowed down greatly.
\par }{\QB I go mourning all day long.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}For my waist is filled with burning.
\par }{\QB There is no soundness in my flesh.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}I am faint and severely bruised.
\par }{\QB I have groaned by reason of the anguish of my heart.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Lord, all my desire is before you.
\par }{\QB My groaning is not hidden from you.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}My heart throbs.
\par }{\QB My strength fails me.
\par }{\QB As for the light of my eyes, it has also left me.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}My lovers and my friends stand aloof from my plague.
\par }{\QB My kinsmen stand far away.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}They also who seek after my life lay snares.
\par }{\QB Those who seek my hurt speak mischievous things,
\par }{\QB and meditate deceits all day long.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}But I, as a deaf man, don’t hear.
\par }{\QB I am as a mute man who doesn’t open his mouth.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Yes, I am as a man who doesn’t hear,
\par }{\QB in whose mouth are no reproofs.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}For I hope in you, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB You will answer, Lord my God.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}For I said, “Don’t let them gloat over me,
\par }{\QB or exalt themselves over me when my foot slips.”
\par }{\Q \VS{17}For I am ready to fall.
\par }{\QB My pain is continually before me.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}For I will declare my iniquity.
\par }{\QB I will be sorry for my sin.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}But my enemies are vigorous and many.
\par }{\QB Those who hate me without reason are numerous.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}They who render evil for good are also adversaries to me,
\par }{\QB because I follow what is good.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Don’t forsake me, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB My God, don’t be far from me.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}Hurry to help me,
\par }{\QB Lord, my salvation.

\par }\PsalmChap{39}{\D For the Chief Musician. For Jeduthun. A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}I said, “I will watch my ways, so that I don’t sin with my tongue.
\par }{\QB I will keep my mouth with a bridle while the wicked is before me.”
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I was mute with silence.
\par }{\QB I held my peace, even from good.
\par }{\QB My sorrow was stirred.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}My heart was hot within me.
\par }{\QB While I meditated, the fire burned.
\par }{\Q I spoke with my tongue:
\par }{\QB \VS{4}“Yahweh, show me my end,
\par }{\QB what is the measure of my days.
\par }{\QB Let me know how frail I am.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Behold, you have made my days hand widths.
\par }{\QB My lifetime is as nothing before you.
\par }{\Q Surely every man stands as a breath.”
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{6}“Surely every man walks like a shadow.
\par }{\QB Surely they busy themselves in vain.
\par }{\QB He heaps up, and doesn’t know who shall gather.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Now, Lord, what do I wait for?
\par }{\QB My hope is in you.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Deliver me from all my transgressions.
\par }{\QB Don’t make me the reproach of the foolish.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}I was mute.
\par }{\QB I didn’t open my mouth,
\par }{\QB because you did it.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Remove your scourge away from me.
\par }{\QB I am overcome by the blow of your hand.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}When you rebuke and correct man for iniquity,
\par }{\QB you consume his wealth like a moth.
\par }{\Q Surely every man is but a breath.”
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{12}“Hear my prayer, Yahweh, and give ear to my cry.
\par }{\QB Don’t be silent at my tears.
\par }{\Q For I am a stranger with you,
\par }{\QB a foreigner, as all my fathers were.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Oh spare me, that I may recover strength,
\par }{\QB before I go away and exist no more.”

\par }\PsalmChap{40}{\D For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}I waited patiently for Yahweh.
\par }{\QB He turned to me, and heard my cry.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}He brought me up also out of a horrible pit,
\par }{\QB out of the miry clay.
\par }{\Q He set my feet on a rock,
\par }{\QB and gave me a firm place to stand.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}He has put a new song in my mouth, even praise to our God.
\par }{\QB Many shall see it, and fear, and shall trust in Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Blessed is the man who makes Yahweh his trust,
\par }{\QB and doesn’t respect the proud, nor such as turn away to lies.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Many, Yahweh, my God, are the wonderful works which you have done,
\par }{\QB and your thoughts which are toward us.
\par }{\Q They can’t be declared back to you.
\par }{\QB If I would declare and speak of them, they are more than can be counted.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Sacrifice and offering you didn’t desire.
\par }{\QB You have opened my ears.
\par }{\QB You have not required burnt offering and sin offering.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Then I said, “Behold, I have come.
\par }{\QB It is written about me in the book in the scroll.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}I delight to do your will, my God.
\par }{\QB Yes, your law is within my heart.”
\par }{\Q \VS{9}I have proclaimed glad news of righteousness in the great assembly.
\par }{\QB Behold, I will not seal my lips, Yahweh, you know.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}I have not hidden your righteousness within my heart.
\par }{\QB I have declared your faithfulness and your salvation.
\par }{\QB I have not concealed your loving kindness and your truth from the great assembly.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Don’t withhold your tender mercies from me, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB Let your loving kindness and your truth continually preserve me.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}For innumerable evils have surrounded me.
\par }{\QB My iniquities have overtaken me, so that I am not able to look up.
\par }{\Q They are more than the hairs of my head.
\par }{\QB My heart has failed me.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Be pleased, Yahweh, to deliver me.
\par }{\QB Hurry to help me, Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Let them be disappointed and confounded together who seek after my soul to destroy it.
\par }{\QB Let them be turned backward and brought to dishonor who delight in my hurt.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Let them be desolate by reason of their shame that tell me, “Aha! Aha!”
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Let all those who seek you rejoice and be glad in you.
\par }{\QB Let such as love your salvation say continually, “Let Yahweh be exalted!”
\par }{\Q \VS{17}But I am poor and needy.
\par }{\QB May the Lord think about me.
\par }{\Q You are my help and my deliverer.
\par }{\QB Don’t delay, my God.

\par }\PsalmChap{41}{\D For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Blessed is he who considers the poor.
\par }{\QB Yahweh will deliver him in the day of evil.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Yahweh will preserve him, and keep him alive.
\par }{\QB He shall be blessed on the earth,
\par }{\QB and he will not surrender him to the will of his enemies.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Yahweh will sustain him on his sickbed,
\par }{\QB and restore him from his bed of illness.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}I said, “Yahweh, have mercy on me!
\par }{\QB Heal me, for I have sinned against you.”
\par }{\Q \VS{5}My enemies speak evil against me:
\par }{\QB “When will he die, and his name perish?”
\par }{\Q \VS{6}If he comes to see me, he speaks falsehood.
\par }{\QB His heart gathers iniquity to itself.
\par }{\QB When he goes abroad, he tells it.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}All who hate me whisper together against me.
\par }{\QB They imagine the worst for me.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}“An evil disease”, they say, “has afflicted him.
\par }{\QB Now that he lies he shall rise up no more.”
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Yes, my own familiar friend, in whom I trusted,
\par }{\QB who ate bread with me,
\par }{\QB has lifted up his heel against me.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{10}But you, Yahweh, have mercy on me, and raise me up,
\par }{\QB that I may repay them.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}By this I know that you delight in me,
\par }{\QB because my enemy doesn’t triumph over me.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}As for me, you uphold me in my integrity,
\par }{\QB and set me in your presence forever.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{13}Blessed be Yahweh, the God of Israel,
\par }{\QB from everlasting and to everlasting!
\par }{\Q Amen and amen.

\par }\PsalmChap{42}{\D For the Chief Musician. A contemplation by the sons of Korah.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}As the deer pants for the water brooks,
\par }{\QB so my soul pants after you, God.\FTNT{*}{{\FR 42:1 }
The Hebrew word rendered “God” is “אֱלֹהִ֑ים” (Elohim).}
\par }{\Q \VS{2}My soul thirsts for God, for the living God.
\par }{\QB When shall I come and appear before God?
\par }{\Q \VS{3}My tears have been my food day and night,
\par }{\QB while they continually ask me, “Where is your God?”
\par }{\Q \VS{4}These things I remember, and pour out my soul within me,
\par }{\QB how I used to go with the crowd, and led them to God’s house,
\par }{\QB with the voice of joy and praise, a multitude keeping a holy day.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Why are you in despair, my soul?
\par }{\QB Why are you disturbed within me?
\par }{\Q Hope in God!
\par }{\QB For I shall still praise him for the saving help of his presence.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}My God, my soul is in despair within me.
\par }{\QB Therefore I remember you from the land of the Jordan,
\par }{\QB the heights of Hermon, from the hill Mizar.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Deep calls to deep at the noise of your waterfalls.
\par }{\QB All your waves and your billows have swept over me.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{8}Yahweh\FTNT{†}{{\FR 42:8 }
“Yahweh” is God’s proper Name, sometimes rendered “LORD” (all caps) in other translations.} will command his loving kindness in the daytime.
\par }{\QB In the night his song shall be with me:
\par }{\QB a prayer to the God of my life.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}I will ask God, my rock, “Why have you forgotten me?
\par }{\QB Why do I go mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?”
\par }{\Q \VS{10}As with a sword in my bones, my adversaries reproach me,
\par }{\QB while they continually ask me, “Where is your God?”
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Why are you in despair, my soul?
\par }{\QB Why are you disturbed within me?
\par }{\Q Hope in God! For I shall still praise him,
\par }{\QB the saving help of my countenance, and my God.

\par }\PsalmChap{43}{\Q \VerseOne{1}Vindicate me, God, and plead my cause against an ungodly nation.
\par }{\QB Oh, deliver me from deceitful and wicked men.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}For you are the God of my strength. Why have you rejected me?
\par }{\QB Why do I go mourning because of the oppression of the enemy?
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Oh, send out your light and your truth.
\par }{\QB Let them lead me.
\par }{\QB Let them bring me to your holy hill,
\par }{\QB to your tents.

\par }{\QB to God, my exceeding joy.
\par }{\Q I will praise you on the harp, God, my God.

\par }{\QB Why are you disturbed within me?
\par }{\Q Hope in God!
\par }{\QB For I shall still praise him:
\par }{\QB my Savior, my helper, and my God.

\par }\PsalmChap{44}{\D For the Chief Musician. By the sons of Korah. A contemplative psalm.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}We have heard with our ears, God;
\par }{\QB our fathers have told us what work you did in their days,
\par }{\QB in the days of old.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}You drove out the nations with your hand,
\par }{\QB but you planted them.
\par }{\Q You afflicted the peoples,
\par }{\QB but you spread them abroad.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For they didn’t get the land in possession by their own sword,
\par }{\QB neither did their own arm save them;
\par }{\Q but your right hand, your arm, and the light of your face,
\par }{\QB because you were favorable to them.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}You are my King, God.
\par }{\QB Command victories for Jacob!
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Through you, will we push down our adversaries.
\par }{\QB Through your name, we will tread down those who rise up against us.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}For I will not trust in my bow,
\par }{\QB neither shall my sword save me.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}But you have saved us from our adversaries,
\par }{\QB and have shamed those who hate us.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}In God we have made our boast all day long,
\par }{\QB we will give thanks to your name forever.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{9}But now you rejected us, and brought us to dishonor,
\par }{\QB and don’t go out with our armies.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}You make us turn back from the adversary.
\par }{\QB Those who hate us take plunder for themselves.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}You have made us like sheep for food,
\par }{\QB and have scattered us among the nations.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}You sell your people for nothing,
\par }{\QB and have gained nothing from their sale.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}You make us a reproach to our neighbors,
\par }{\QB a scoffing and a derision to those who are around us.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}You make us a byword among the nations,
\par }{\QB a shaking of the head among the peoples.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}All day long my dishonor is before me,
\par }{\QB and shame covers my face,
\par }{\QB \VS{16}at the taunt of one who reproaches and verbally abuses,
\par }{\QB because of the enemy and the avenger.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}All this has come on us,
\par }{\QB yet we haven’t forgotten you.
\par }{\QB We haven’t been false to your covenant.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Our heart has not turned back,
\par }{\QB neither have our steps strayed from your path,
\par }{\QB \VS{19}though you have crushed us in the haunt of jackals,
\par }{\QB and covered us with the shadow of death.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}If we have forgotten the name of our God,
\par }{\QB or spread out our hands to a strange god,
\par }{\QB \VS{21}won’t God search this out?
\par }{\QB For he knows the secrets of the heart.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}Yes, for your sake we are killed all day long.
\par }{\QB We are regarded as sheep for the slaughter.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Wake up!
\par }{\QB Why do you sleep, Lord?\FTNT{*}{{\FR 44:23 }
The word translated “Lord” is “Adonai.”
}
\par }{\Q Arise!
\par }{\QB Don’t reject us forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}Why do you hide your face,
\par }{\QB and forget our affliction and our oppression?
\par }{\Q \VS{25}For our soul is bowed down to the dust.
\par }{\QB Our body clings to the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}Rise up to help us.
\par }{\QB Redeem us for your loving kindness’ sake.

\par }\PsalmChap{45}{\D For the Chief Musician. Set to “The Lilies.” A contemplation by the sons of Korah. A wedding song.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}My heart overflows with a noble theme.
\par }{\QB I recite my verses for the king.
\par }{\QB My tongue is like the pen of a skillful writer.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}You are the most excellent of the sons of men.
\par }{\QB Grace has anointed your lips,
\par }{\QB therefore God has blessed you forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Strap your sword on your thigh, mighty one:
\par }{\QB your splendor and your majesty.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}In your majesty ride on victoriously on behalf of truth, humility, and righteousness.
\par }{\QB Let your right hand display awesome deeds.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Your arrows are sharp.
\par }{\QB The nations fall under you, with arrows in the heart of the king’s enemies.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Your throne, God, is forever and ever.
\par }{\QB A scepter of equity is the scepter of your kingdom.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}You have loved righteousness, and hated wickedness.
\par }{\QB Therefore God, your God, has anointed you with the oil of gladness above your fellows.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}All your garments smell like myrrh, aloes, and cassia.
\par }{\QB Out of ivory palaces stringed instruments have made you glad.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Kings’ daughters are among your honorable women.
\par }{\QB At your right hand the queen stands in gold of Ophir.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Listen, daughter, consider, and turn your ear.
\par }{\QB Forget your own people, and also your father’s house.
\par }{\QB \VS{11}So the king will desire your beauty,
\par }{\QB honor him, for he is your lord.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}The daughter of Tyre comes with a gift.
\par }{\QB The rich among the people entreat your favor.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}The princess inside is all glorious.
\par }{\QB Her clothing is interwoven with gold.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}She shall be led to the king in embroidered work.
\par }{\QB The virgins, her companions who follow her, shall be brought to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}With gladness and rejoicing they shall be led.
\par }{\QB They shall enter into the king’s palace.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Your sons will take the place of your fathers.
\par }{\QB You shall make them princes in all the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}I will make your name to be remembered in all generations.
\par }{\QB Therefore the peoples shall give you thanks forever and ever.
