\par }\PsalmChap{48}{\D A Song. A Psalm by the sons of Korah.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Great is Yahweh, and greatly to be praised,
\par }{\QB in the city of our God, in his holy mountain.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Beautiful in elevation, the joy of the whole earth,
\par }{\QB is Mount Zion, on the north sides,
\par }{\QB the city of the great King.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}God has shown himself in her citadels as a refuge.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For, behold, the kings assembled themselves,
\par }{\QB they passed by together.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They saw it, then they were amazed.
\par }{\QB They were dismayed.
\par }{\QB They hurried away.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Trembling took hold of them there,
\par }{\QB pain, as of a woman in travail.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}With the east wind, you break the ships of Tarshish.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}As we have heard, so we have seen,
\par }{\QB in the city of Yahweh of Armies, in the city of our God.
\par }{\Q God will establish it forever.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{9}We have thought about your loving kindness, God,
\par }{\QB in the middle of your temple.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}As is your name, God,
\par }{\QB so is your praise to the ends of the earth.
\par }{\QB Your right hand is full of righteousness.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Let Mount Zion be glad!
\par }{\QB Let the daughters of Judah rejoice because of your judgments.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Walk about Zion, and go around her.
\par }{\QB Number its towers.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Notice her bulwarks.
\par }{\QB Consider her palaces,
\par }{\QB that you may tell it to the next generation.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}For this God is our God forever and ever.
\par }{\QB He will be our guide even to death.

\par }\PsalmChap{49}{\D For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by the sons of Korah.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Hear this, all you peoples.
\par }{\QB Listen, all you inhabitants of the world,
\par }{\QB \VS{2}both low and high,
\par }{\QB rich and poor together.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}My mouth will speak words of wisdom.
\par }{\QB My heart will utter understanding.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}I will incline my ear to a proverb.
\par }{\QB I will solve my riddle on the harp.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Why should I fear in the days of evil,
\par }{\QB when iniquity at my heels surrounds me?
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Those who trust in their wealth,
\par }{\QB and boast in the multitude of their riches—
\par }{\QB \VS{7}none of them can by any means redeem his brother,
\par }{\QB nor give God a ransom for him.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}For the redemption of their life is costly,
\par }{\QB no payment is ever enough,
\par }{\QB \VS{9}that he should live on forever,
\par }{\QB that he should not see corruption.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}For he sees that wise men die;
\par }{\QB likewise the fool and the senseless perish,
\par }{\QB and leave their wealth to others.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Their inward thought is that their houses will endure forever,
\par }{\QB and their dwelling places to all generations.
\par }{\QB They name their lands after themselves.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}But man, despite his riches, doesn’t endure.
\par }{\QB He is like the animals that perish.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{13}This is the destiny of those who are foolish,
\par }{\QB and of those who approve their sayings.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{14}They are appointed as a flock for Sheol.\FTNT{*}{{\FR 49:14 }
Sheol is the place of the dead.}
\par }{\QB Death shall be their shepherd.
\par }{\Q The upright shall have dominion over them in the morning.
\par }{\QB Their beauty shall decay in Sheol,\FTNT{†}{{\FR 49:14 }
Sheol is the place of the dead.
}
\par }{\QB far from their mansion.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}But God will redeem my soul from the power of Sheol,\FTNT{‡}{{\FR 49:15 }
Sheol is the place of the dead.}
\par }{\QB for he will receive me.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{16}Don’t be afraid when a man is made rich,
\par }{\QB when the glory of his house is increased;
\par }{\Q \VS{17}for when he dies he will carry nothing away.
\par }{\QB His glory won’t descend after him.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Though while he lived he blessed his soul—
\par }{\QB and men praise you when you do well for yourself—
\par }{\QB \VS{19}he shall go to the generation of his fathers.
\par }{\QB They shall never see the light.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}A man who has riches without understanding,
\par }{\QB is like the animals that perish.

\par }\PsalmChap{50}{\D A Psalm by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}The Mighty One, God, Yahweh, speaks,
\par }{\QB and calls the earth from sunrise to sunset.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Out of Zion, the perfection of beauty,
\par }{\QB God shines out.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Our God comes, and does not keep silent.
\par }{\QB A fire devours before him.
\par }{\QB It is very stormy around him.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}He calls to the heavens above,
\par }{\QB to the earth, that he may judge his people:
\par }{\Q \VS{5}“Gather my saints together to me,
\par }{\QB those who have made a covenant with me by sacrifice.”
\par }{\Q \VS{6}The heavens shall declare his righteousness,
\par }{\QB for God himself is judge.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{7}“Hear, my people, and I will speak.
\par }{\QB Israel, I will testify against you.
\par }{\Q I am God, your God.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}I don’t rebuke you for your sacrifices.
\par }{\QB Your burnt offerings are continually before me.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}I have no need for a bull from your stall,
\par }{\QB nor male goats from your pens.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}For every animal of the forest is mine,
\par }{\QB and the livestock on a thousand hills.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}I know all the birds of the mountains.
\par }{\QB The wild animals of the field are mine.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}If I were hungry, I would not tell you,
\par }{\QB for the world is mine, and all that is in it.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Will I eat the meat of bulls,
\par }{\QB or drink the blood of goats?
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Offer to God the sacrifice of thanksgiving.
\par }{\QB Pay your vows to the Most High.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Call on me in the day of trouble.
\par }{\QB I will deliver you, and you will honor me.”
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{16}But to the wicked God says,
\par }{\QB “What right do you have to declare my statutes,
\par }{\QB that you have taken my covenant on your lips,
\par }{\QB \VS{17}since you hate instruction,
\par }{\QB and throw my words behind you?
\par }{\Q \VS{18}When you saw a thief, you consented with him,
\par }{\QB and have participated with adulterers.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{19}“You give your mouth to evil.
\par }{\QB Your tongue frames deceit.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}You sit and speak against your brother.
\par }{\QB You slander your own mother’s son.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}You have done these things, and I kept silent.
\par }{\QB You thought that I was just like you.
\par }{\QB I will rebuke you, and accuse you in front of your eyes.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{22}“Now consider this, you who forget God,
\par }{\QB lest I tear you into pieces, and there be no one to deliver.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Whoever offers the sacrifice of thanksgiving glorifies me,
\par }{\QB and prepares his way so that I will show God’s salvation to him.”

\par }\PsalmChap{51}{\D For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David, when Nathan the prophet came to him, after he had gone in to Bathsheba.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Have mercy on me, God, according to your loving kindness.
\par }{\QB According to the multitude of your tender mercies, blot out my transgressions.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Wash me thoroughly from my iniquity.
\par }{\QB Cleanse me from my sin.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For I know my transgressions.
\par }{\QB My sin is constantly before me.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Against you, and you only, I have sinned,
\par }{\QB and done that which is evil in your sight,
\par }{\Q so you may be proved right when you speak,
\par }{\QB and justified when you judge.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Behold, I was born in iniquity.
\par }{\QB My mother conceived me in sin.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Behold, you desire truth in the inward parts.
\par }{\QB You teach me wisdom in the inmost place.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Purify me with hyssop, and I will be clean.
\par }{\QB Wash me, and I will be whiter than snow.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Let me hear joy and gladness,
\par }{\QB that the bones which you have broken may rejoice.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Hide your face from my sins,
\par }{\QB and blot out all of my iniquities.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Create in me a clean heart, O God.
\par }{\QB Renew a right spirit within me.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Don’t throw me from your presence,
\par }{\QB and don’t take your Holy Spirit from me.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Restore to me the joy of your salvation.
\par }{\QB Uphold me with a willing spirit.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Then I will teach transgressors your ways.
\par }{\QB Sinners will be converted to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Deliver me from the guilt of bloodshed, O God, the God of my salvation.
\par }{\QB My tongue will sing aloud of your righteousness.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Lord, open my lips.
\par }{\QB My mouth will declare your praise.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}For you don’t delight in sacrifice, or else I would give it.
\par }{\QB You have no pleasure in burnt offering.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}The sacrifices of God are a broken spirit.
\par }{\QB O God, you will not despise a broken and contrite heart.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{18}Do well in your good pleasure to Zion.
\par }{\QB Build the walls of Jerusalem.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Then you will delight in the sacrifices of righteousness,
\par }{\QB in burnt offerings and in whole burnt offerings.
\par }{\Q Then they will offer bulls on your altar.

\par }\PsalmChap{52}{\D For the Chief Musician. A contemplation by David, when Doeg the Edomite came and told Saul, “David has come to Ahimelech’s house.”
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Why do you boast of mischief, mighty man?
\par }{\QB God’s loving kindness endures continually.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Your tongue plots destruction,
\par }{\QB like a sharp razor, working deceitfully.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}You love evil more than good,
\par }{\QB lying rather than speaking the truth.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{4}You love all devouring words,
\par }{\QB you deceitful tongue.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}God will likewise destroy you forever.
\par }{\QB He will take you up, and pluck you out of your tent,
\par }{\QB and root you out of the land of the living.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{6}The righteous also will see it, and fear,
\par }{\QB and laugh at him, saying,
\par }{\Q \VS{7}“Behold, this is the man who didn’t make God his strength,
\par }{\QB but trusted in the abundance of his riches,
\par }{\QB and strengthened himself in his wickedness.”
\par }{\Q \VS{8}But as for me, I am like a green olive tree in God’s house.
\par }{\QB I trust in God’s loving kindness forever and ever.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}I will give you thanks forever, because you have done it.
\par }{\QB I will hope in your name, for it is good,
\par }{\QB in the presence of your saints.

\par }\PsalmChap{53}{\D For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Mahalath.” A contemplation by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}The fool has said in his heart, “There is no God.”
\par }{\QB They are corrupt, and have done abominable iniquity.
\par }{\QB There is no one who does good.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}God looks down from heaven on the children of men,
\par }{\QB to see if there are any who understood,
\par }{\QB who seek after God.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Every one of them has gone back.
\par }{\QB They have become filthy together.
\par }{\QB There is no one who does good, no, not one.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Have the workers of iniquity no knowledge,
\par }{\QB who eat up my people as they eat bread,
\par }{\QB and don’t call on God?
\par }{\Q \VS{5}There they were in great fear, where no fear was,
\par }{\QB for God has scattered the bones of him who encamps against you.
\par }{\Q You have put them to shame,
\par }{\QB because God has rejected them.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Oh that the salvation of Israel would come out of Zion!
\par }{\QB When God brings back his people from captivity,
\par }{\QB then Jacob shall rejoice,
\par }{\QB and Israel shall be glad.

\par }\PsalmChap{54}{\D For the Chief Musician. On stringed instruments. A contemplation by David, when the Ziphites came and said to Saul, “Isn’t David hiding himself among us?”
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Save me, God, by your name.
\par }{\QB Vindicate me in your might.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Hear my prayer, God.
\par }{\QB Listen to the words of my mouth.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For strangers have risen up against me.
\par }{\QB Violent men have sought after my soul.
\par }{\QB They haven’t set God before them.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{4}Behold, God is my helper.
\par }{\QB The Lord is the one who sustains my soul.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}He will repay the evil to my enemies.
\par }{\QB Destroy them in your truth.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}With a free will offering, I will sacrifice to you.
\par }{\QB I will give thanks to your name, Yahweh, for it is good.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}For he has delivered me out of all trouble.
\par }{\QB My eye has seen triumph over my enemies.

\par }\PsalmChap{55}{\D For the Chief Musician. On stringed instruments. A contemplation by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Listen to my prayer, God.
\par }{\QB Don’t hide yourself from my supplication.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Attend to me, and answer me.
\par }{\QB I am restless in my complaint,
\par }{\QB and moan
\VS{3}because of the voice of the enemy,
\par }{\QB because of the oppression of the wicked.
\par }{\Q For they bring suffering on me.
\par }{\QB In anger they hold a grudge against me.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}My heart is severely pained within me.
\par }{\QB The terrors of death have fallen on me.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Fearfulness and trembling have come on me.
\par }{\QB Horror has overwhelmed me.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I said, “Oh that I had wings like a dove!
\par }{\QB Then I would fly away, and be at rest.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Behold, then I would wander far off.
\par }{\QB I would lodge in the wilderness.”
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{8}“I would hurry to a shelter from the stormy wind and storm.”
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Confuse them, Lord, and confound their language,
\par }{\QB for I have seen violence and strife in the city.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Day and night they prowl around on its walls.
\par }{\QB Malice and abuse are also within her.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Destructive forces are within her.
\par }{\QB Threats and lies don’t depart from her streets.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}For it was not an enemy who insulted me,
\par }{\QB then I could have endured it.
\par }{\Q Neither was it he who hated me who raised himself up against me,
\par }{\QB then I would have hidden myself from him.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}But it was you, a man like me,
\par }{\QB my companion, and my familiar friend.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}We took sweet fellowship together.
\par }{\QB We walked in God’s house with company.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Let death come suddenly on them.
\par }{\QB Let them go down alive into Sheol.\FTNT{*}{{\FR 55:15 }
Sheol is the place of the dead.
}
\par }{\QB For wickedness is among them, in their dwelling.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}As for me, I will call on God.
\par }{\QB Yahweh will save me.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Evening, morning, and at noon, I will cry out in distress.
\par }{\QB He will hear my voice.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}He has redeemed my soul in peace from the battle that was against me,
\par }{\QB although there are many who oppose me.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}God, who is enthroned forever,
\par }{\QB will hear and answer them.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\BB \par }{\Q They never change,
\par }{\QB who don’t fear God.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}He raises his hands against his friends.
\par }{\QB He has violated his covenant.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}His mouth was smooth as butter,
\par }{\QB but his heart was war.
\par }{\Q His words were softer than oil,
\par }{\QB yet they were drawn swords.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{22}Cast your burden on Yahweh and he will sustain you.
\par }{\QB He will never allow the righteous to be moved.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}But you, God, will bring them down into the pit of destruction.
\par }{\QB Bloodthirsty and deceitful men shall not live out half their days,
\par }{\QB but I will trust in you.

\par }\PsalmChap{56}{\D For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Silent Dove in Distant Lands.” A poem by David, when the Philistines seized him in Gath.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Be merciful to me, God, for man wants to swallow me up.
\par }{\QB All day long, he attacks and oppresses me.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}My enemies want to swallow me up all day long,
\par }{\QB for they are many who fight proudly against me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}When I am afraid,
\par }{\QB I will put my trust in you.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}In God, I praise his word.
\par }{\QB In God, I put my trust.
\par }{\Q I will not be afraid.
\par }{\QB What can flesh do to me?
\par }{\Q \VS{5}All day long they twist my words.
\par }{\QB All their thoughts are against me for evil.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}They conspire and lurk,
\par }{\QB watching my steps.
\par }{\QB They are eager to take my life.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Shall they escape by iniquity?
\par }{\QB In anger cast down the peoples, God.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}You count my wanderings.
\par }{\QB You put my tears into your container.
\par }{\QB Aren’t they in your book?
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Then my enemies shall turn back in the day that I call.
\par }{\QB I know this: that God is for me.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}In God, I will praise his word.
\par }{\QB In Yahweh, I will praise his word.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}I have put my trust in God.
\par }{\QB I will not be afraid.
\par }{\QB What can man do to me?
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Your vows are on me, God.
\par }{\QB I will give thank offerings to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}For you have delivered my soul from death,
\par }{\QB and prevented my feet from falling,
\par }{\QB that I may walk before God in the light of the living.

\par }\PsalmChap{57}{\D For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A poem by David, when he fled from Saul, in the cave.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Be merciful to me, God, be merciful to me,
\par }{\QB for my soul takes refuge in you.
\par }{\Q Yes, in the shadow of your wings, I will take refuge,
\par }{\QB until disaster has passed.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I cry out to God Most High,
\par }{\Q to God who accomplishes my requests for me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}He will send from heaven, and save me,
\par }{\QB he rebukes the one who is pursuing me.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q God will send out his loving kindness and his truth.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}My soul is among lions.
\par }{\QB I lie among those who are set on fire,
\par }{\QB even the sons of men, whose teeth are spears and arrows,
\par }{\QB and their tongue a sharp sword.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Be exalted, God, above the heavens!
\par }{\QB Let your glory be above all the earth!
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{6}They have prepared a net for my steps.
\par }{\QB My soul is bowed down.
\par }{\Q They dig a pit before me.
\par }{\QB They fall into the middle of it themselves.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{7}My heart is steadfast, God.
\par }{\QB My heart is steadfast.
\par }{\QB I will sing, yes, I will sing praises.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Wake up, my glory! Wake up, lute and harp!
\par }{\QB I will wake up the dawn.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}I will give thanks to you, Lord, among the peoples.
\par }{\QB I will sing praises to you among the nations.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}For your great loving kindness reaches to the heavens,
\par }{\QB and your truth to the skies.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Be exalted, God, above the heavens.
\par }{\QB Let your glory be over all the earth.

\par }\PsalmChap{58}{\D For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A poem by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Do you indeed speak righteousness, silent ones?
\par }{\QB Do you judge blamelessly, you sons of men?
\par }{\Q \VS{2}No, in your heart you plot injustice.
\par }{\QB You measure out the violence of your hands in the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}The wicked go astray from the womb.
\par }{\QB They are wayward as soon as they are born, speaking lies.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Their poison is like the poison of a snake,
\par }{\QB like a deaf cobra that stops its ear,
\par }{\QB \VS{5}which doesn’t listen to the voice of charmers,
\par }{\QB no matter how skillful the charmer may be.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Break their teeth, God, in their mouth.
\par }{\QB Break out the great teeth of the young lions, Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Let them vanish like water that flows away.
\par }{\QB When they draw the bow, let their arrows be made blunt.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Let them be like a snail which melts and passes away,
\par }{\QB like the stillborn child, who has not seen the sun.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Before your pots can feel the heat of the thorns,
\par }{\QB he will sweep away the green and the burning alike.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}The righteous shall rejoice when he sees the vengeance.
\par }{\QB He shall wash his feet in the blood of the wicked,
\par }{\Q \VS{11}so that men shall say, “Most certainly there is a reward for the righteous.
\par }{\QB Most certainly there is a God who judges the earth.”

\par }\PsalmChap{59}{\D For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A poem by David, when Saul sent, and they watched the house to kill him.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Deliver me from my enemies, my God.
\par }{\QB Set me on high from those who rise up against me.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Deliver me from the workers of iniquity.
\par }{\QB Save me from the bloodthirsty men.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For, behold, they lie in wait for my soul.
\par }{\QB The mighty gather themselves together against me,
\par }{\QB not for my disobedience, nor for my sin, Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}I have done no wrong, yet they are ready to attack me.
\par }{\QB Rise up, behold, and help me!
\par }{\Q \VS{5}You, Yahweh God of Armies, the God of Israel,
\par }{\QB rouse yourself to punish the nations.
\par }{\QB Show no mercy to the wicked traitors.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{6}They return at evening, howling like dogs,
\par }{\QB and prowl around the city.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Behold, they spew with their mouth.
\par }{\QB Swords are in their lips,
\par }{\QB “For”, they say, “who hears us?”
\par }{\Q \VS{8}But you, Yahweh, laugh at them.
\par }{\QB You scoff at all the nations.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Oh, my Strength, I watch for you,
\par }{\QB for God is my high tower.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}My God will go before me with his loving kindness.
\par }{\QB God will let me look at my enemies in triumph.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Don’t kill them, or my people may forget.
\par }{\QB Scatter them by your power, and bring them down, Lord our shield.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}For the sin of their mouth, and the words of their lips,
\par }{\QB let them be caught in their pride,
\par }{\QB for the curses and lies which they utter.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Consume them in wrath.
\par }{\QB Consume them, and they will be no more.
\par }{\Q Let them know that God rules in Jacob,
\par }{\QB to the ends of the earth.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{14}At evening let them return.
\par }{\QB Let them howl like a dog, and go around the city.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}They shall wander up and down for food,
\par }{\QB and wait all night if they aren’t satisfied.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{16}But I will sing of your strength.
\par }{\QB Yes, I will sing aloud of your loving kindness in the morning.
\par }{\Q For you have been my high tower,
\par }{\QB a refuge in the day of my distress.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}To you, my strength, I will sing praises.
\par }{\QB For God is my high tower, the God of my mercy.

\par }\PsalmChap{60}{\D For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “The Lily of the Covenant.” A teaching poem by David, when he fought with Aram Naharaim and with Aram Zobah, and Joab returned, and killed twelve thousand of Edom in the Valley of Salt.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}God, you have rejected us.
\par }{\QB You have broken us down.
\par }{\Q You have been angry.
\par }{\QB Restore us, again.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}You have made the land tremble.
\par }{\QB You have torn it.
\par }{\Q Mend its fractures,
\par }{\QB for it quakes.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}You have shown your people hard things.
\par }{\QB You have made us drink the wine that makes us stagger.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}You have given a banner to those who fear you,
\par }{\QB that it may be displayed because of the truth.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{5}So that your beloved may be delivered,
\par }{\QB save with your right hand, and answer us.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}God has spoken from his sanctuary:
\par }{\QB “I will triumph.
\par }{\QB I will divide Shechem,
\par }{\QB and measure out the valley of Succoth.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Gilead is mine, and Manasseh is mine.
\par }{\QB Ephraim also is the defense of my head.
\par }{\QB Judah is my scepter.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Moab is my wash basin.
\par }{\QB I will throw my sandal on Edom.
\par }{\QB I shout in triumph over Philistia.”
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{9}Who will bring me into the strong city?
\par }{\QB Who has led me to Edom?
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Haven’t you, God, rejected us?
\par }{\QB You don’t go out with our armies, God.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Give us help against the adversary,
\par }{\QB for the help of man is vain.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Through God we will do valiantly,
\par }{\QB for it is he who will tread down our adversaries.

\par }\PsalmChap{61}{\D For the Chief Musician. For a stringed instrument. By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Hear my cry, God.
\par }{\QB Listen to my prayer.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}From the end of the earth, I will call to you when my heart is overwhelmed.
\par }{\QB Lead me to the rock that is higher than I.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For you have been a refuge for me,
\par }{\QB a strong tower from the enemy.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}I will dwell in your tent forever.
\par }{\QB I will take refuge in the shelter of your wings.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{5}For you, God, have heard my vows.
\par }{\QB You have given me the heritage of those who fear your name.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}You will prolong the king’s life.
\par }{\QB His years will be for generations.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}He shall be enthroned in God’s presence forever.
\par }{\QB Appoint your loving kindness and truth, that they may preserve him.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}So I will sing praise to your name forever,
\par }{\QB that I may fulfill my vows daily.

\par }\PsalmChap{62}{\D For the Chief Musician. To Jeduthun. A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}My soul rests in God alone.
\par }{\QB My salvation is from him.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}He alone is my rock, my salvation, and my fortress.
\par }{\QB I will never be greatly shaken.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}How long will you assault a man?
\par }{\QB Would all of you throw him down,
\par }{\QB like a leaning wall, like a tottering fence?
\par }{\Q \VS{4}They fully intend to throw him down from his lofty place.
\par }{\QB They delight in lies.
\par }{\QB They bless with their mouth, but they curse inwardly.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{5}My soul, wait in silence for God alone,
\par }{\QB for my expectation is from him.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}He alone is my rock and my salvation, my fortress.
\par }{\QB I will not be shaken.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}My salvation and my honor is with God.
\par }{\QB The rock of my strength, and my refuge, is in God.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Trust in him at all times, you people.
\par }{\QB Pour out your heart before him.
\par }{\QB God is a refuge for us.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{9}Surely men of low degree are just a breath,
\par }{\QB and men of high degree are a lie.
\par }{\Q In the balances they will go up.
\par }{\QB They are together lighter than a breath.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Don’t trust in oppression.
\par }{\QB Don’t become vain in robbery.
\par }{\Q If riches increase,
\par }{\QB don’t set your heart on them.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}God has spoken once;
\par }{\QB twice I have heard this,
\par }{\QB that power belongs to God.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Also to you, Lord, belongs loving kindness,
\par }{\QB for you reward every man according to his work.

\par }\PsalmChap{63}{\D A Psalm by David, when he was in the desert of Judah.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}God, you are my God.
\par }{\QB I will earnestly seek you.
\par }{\Q My soul thirsts for you.
\par }{\QB My flesh longs for you,
\par }{\QB in a dry and weary land, where there is no water.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}So I have seen you in the sanctuary,
\par }{\QB watching your power and your glory.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Because your loving kindness is better than life,
\par }{\QB my lips shall praise you.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}So I will bless you while I live.
\par }{\QB I will lift up my hands in your name.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}My soul shall be satisfied as with the richest food.
\par }{\QB My mouth shall praise you with joyful lips,
\par }{\QB \VS{6}when I remember you on my bed,
\par }{\QB and think about you in the night watches.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}For you have been my help.
\par }{\QB I will rejoice in the shadow of your wings.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}My soul stays close to you.
\par }{\QB Your right hand holds me up.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}But those who seek my soul to destroy it
\par }{\QB shall go into the lower parts of the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}They shall be given over to the power of the sword.
\par }{\QB They shall be jackal food.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}But the king shall rejoice in God.
\par }{\QB Everyone who swears by him will praise him,
\par }{\QB for the mouth of those who speak lies shall be silenced.

\par }\PsalmChap{64}{\D For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Hear my voice, God, in my complaint.
\par }{\QB Preserve my life from fear of the enemy.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Hide me from the conspiracy of the wicked,
\par }{\QB from the noisy crowd of the ones doing evil;
\par }{\Q \VS{3}who sharpen their tongue like a sword,
\par }{\QB and aim their arrows, deadly words,
\par }{\QB \VS{4}to shoot innocent men from ambushes.
\par }{\QB They shoot at him suddenly and fearlessly.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They encourage themselves in evil plans.
\par }{\QB They talk about laying snares secretly.
\par }{\QB They say, “Who will see them?”
\par }{\Q \VS{6}They plot injustice, saying, “We have made a perfect plan!”
\par }{\QB Surely man’s mind and heart are cunning.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}But God will shoot at them.
\par }{\QB They will be suddenly struck down with an arrow.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Their own tongues shall ruin them.
\par }{\QB All who see them will shake their heads.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}All mankind shall be afraid.
\par }{\QB They shall declare the work of God,
\par }{\QB and shall wisely ponder what he has done.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}The righteous shall be glad in Yahweh,
\par }{\QB and shall take refuge in him.
\par }{\QB All the upright in heart shall praise him!

\par }\PsalmChap{65}{\D For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. A song.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Praise waits for you, God, in Zion.
\par }{\QB Vows shall be performed to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}You who hear prayer,
\par }{\QB all men will come to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Sins overwhelmed me,
\par }{\QB but you atoned for our transgressions.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Blessed is the one whom you choose and cause to come near,
\par }{\QB that he may live in your courts.
\par }{\QB We will be filled with the goodness of your house,
\par }{\QB your holy temple.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}By awesome deeds of righteousness, you answer us,
\par }{\QB God of our salvation.
\par }{\Q You who are the hope of all the ends of the earth,
\par }{\QB of those who are far away on the sea.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}By your power, you form the mountains,
\par }{\QB having armed yourself with strength.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}You still the roaring of the seas,
\par }{\QB the roaring of their waves,
\par }{\QB and the turmoil of the nations.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}They also who dwell in faraway places are afraid at your wonders.
\par }{\QB You call the morning’s dawn and the evening with songs of joy.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}You visit the earth, and water it.
\par }{\QB You greatly enrich it.
\par }{\Q The river of God is full of water.
\par }{\QB You provide them grain, for so you have ordained it.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}You drench its furrows.
\par }{\QB You level its ridges.
\par }{\QB You soften it with showers.
\par }{\QB You bless it with a crop.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}You crown the year with your bounty.
\par }{\QB Your carts overflow with abundance.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}The wilderness grasslands overflow.
\par }{\QB The hills are clothed with gladness.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}The pastures are covered with flocks.
\par }{\QB The valleys also are clothed with grain.
\par }{\Q They shout for joy!
\par }{\QB They also sing.

\par }\PsalmChap{66}{\D For the Chief Musician. A song. A Psalm.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Make a joyful shout to God, all the earth!
\par }{\QB \VS{2}Sing to the glory of his name!
\par }{\QB Offer glory and praise!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Tell God, “How awesome are your deeds!
\par }{\QB Through the greatness of your power, your enemies submit themselves to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}All the earth will worship you,
\par }{\QB and will sing to you;
\par }{\QB they will sing to your name.”
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{5}Come, and see God’s deeds—
\par }{\QB awesome work on behalf of the children of men.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}He turned the sea into dry land.
\par }{\QB They went through the river on foot.
\par }{\QB There, we rejoiced in him.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}He rules by his might forever.
\par }{\QB His eyes watch the nations.
\par }{\QB Don’t let the rebellious rise up against him.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{8}Praise our God, you peoples!
\par }{\QB Make the sound of his praise heard,
\par }{\Q \VS{9}who preserves our life among the living,
\par }{\QB and doesn’t allow our feet to be moved.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}For you, God, have tested us.
\par }{\QB You have refined us, as silver is refined.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}You brought us into prison.
\par }{\QB You laid a burden on our backs.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}You allowed men to ride over our heads.
\par }{\QB We went through fire and through water,
\par }{\QB but you brought us to the place of abundance.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}I will come into your temple with burnt offerings.
\par }{\QB I will pay my vows to you,
\VS{14}which my lips promised,
\par }{\QB and my mouth spoke, when I was in distress.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}I will offer to you burnt offerings of fat animals,
\par }{\QB with the offering of rams,
\par }{\QB I will offer bulls with goats.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{16}Come and hear, all you who fear God.
\par }{\QB I will declare what he has done for my soul.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}I cried to him with my mouth.
\par }{\QB He was extolled with my tongue.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}If I cherished sin in my heart,
\par }{\QB the Lord wouldn’t have listened.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}But most certainly, God has listened.
\par }{\QB He has heard the voice of my prayer.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Blessed be God, who has not turned away my prayer,
\par }{\QB nor his loving kindness from me.

\par }\PsalmChap{67}{\D For the Chief Musician. With stringed instruments. A Psalm. A song.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}May God be merciful to us, bless us,
\par }{\QB and cause his face to shine on us.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{2}That your way may be known on earth,
\par }{\QB and your salvation among all nations,
\par }{\Q \VS{3}let the peoples praise you, God.
\par }{\QB Let all the peoples praise you.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Oh let the nations be glad and sing for joy,
\par }{\QB for you will judge the peoples with equity,
\par }{\QB and govern the nations on earth.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{5}Let the peoples praise you, God.
\par }{\QB Let all the peoples praise you.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}The earth has yielded its increase.
\par }{\QB God, even our own God, will bless us.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}God will bless us.
\par }{\QB All the ends of the earth shall fear him.

\par }\PsalmChap{68}{\D For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David. A song.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Let God arise!
\par }{\QB Let his enemies be scattered!
\par }{\QB Let them who hate him also flee before him.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}As smoke is driven away,
\par }{\QB so drive them away.
\par }{\Q As wax melts before the fire,
\par }{\QB so let the wicked perish at the presence of God.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}But let the righteous be glad.
\par }{\QB Let them rejoice before God.
\par }{\QB Yes, let them rejoice with gladness.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Sing to God! Sing praises to his name!
\par }{\QB Extol him who rides on the clouds:
\par }{\Q to Yah, his name!
\par }{\QB Rejoice before him!
\par }{\Q \VS{5}A father of the fatherless, and a defender of the widows,
\par }{\QB is God in his holy habitation.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}God sets the lonely in families.
\par }{\Q He brings out the prisoners with singing,
\par }{\QB but the rebellious dwell in a sun-scorched land.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{7}God, when you went out before your people,
\par }{\QB when you marched through the wilderness...
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{8}The earth trembled.
\par }{\QB The sky also poured down rain at the presence of the God of Sinai—
\par }{\QB at the presence of God, the God of Israel.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}You, God, sent a plentiful rain.
\par }{\QB You confirmed your inheritance when it was weary.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Your congregation lived therein.
\par }{\QB You, God, prepared your goodness for the poor.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}The Lord announced the word.
\par }{\QB The ones who proclaim it are a great company.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}“Kings of armies flee! They flee!”
\par }{\QB She who waits at home divides the plunder,
\par }{\QB \VS{13}while you sleep among the camp fires,
\par }{\QB the wings of a dove sheathed with silver,
\par }{\QB her feathers with shining gold.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}When the Almighty scattered kings in her,
\par }{\QB it snowed on Zalmon.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}The mountains of Bashan are majestic mountains.
\par }{\QB The mountains of Bashan are rugged.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Why do you look in envy, you rugged mountains,
\par }{\QB at the mountain where God chooses to reign?
\par }{\QB Yes, Yahweh will dwell there forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}The chariots of God are tens of thousands and thousands of thousands.
\par }{\QB The Lord is among them, from Sinai, into the sanctuary.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}You have ascended on high.
\par }{\QB You have led away captives.
\par }{\Q You have received gifts among people,
\par }{\QB yes, among the rebellious also, that Yah God might dwell there.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{19}Blessed be the Lord, who daily bears our burdens,
\par }{\QB even the God who is our salvation.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{20}God is to us a God of deliverance.
\par }{\QB To Yahweh, the Lord, belongs escape from death.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}But God will strike through the head of his enemies,
\par }{\QB the hairy scalp of such a one as still continues in his guiltiness.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}The Lord said, “I will bring you again from Bashan,
\par }{\QB I will bring you again from the depths of the sea,
\par }{\Q \VS{23}that you may crush them, dipping your foot in blood,
\par }{\QB that the tongues of your dogs may have their portion from your enemies.”
\par }{\Q \VS{24}They have seen your processions, God,
\par }{\QB even the processions of my God, my King, into the sanctuary.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}The singers went before, the minstrels followed after,
\par }{\QB among the ladies playing with tambourines,
\par }{\Q \VS{26}“Bless God in the congregations,
\par }{\QB even the Lord in the assembly of Israel!”
\par }{\Q \VS{27}There is little Benjamin, their ruler,
\par }{\QB the princes of Judah, their council,
\par }{\QB the princes of Zebulun, and the princes of Naphtali.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{28}Your God has commanded your strength.
\par }{\QB Strengthen, God, that which you have done for us.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}Because of your temple at Jerusalem,
\par }{\QB kings shall bring presents to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{30}Rebuke the wild animal of the reeds,
\par }{\QB the multitude of the bulls, with the calves of the peoples.
\par }{\Q Being humbled, may it bring bars of silver.
\par }{\QB Scatter the nations that delight in war.
\par }{\Q \VS{31}Princes shall come out of Egypt.
\par }{\QB Ethiopia shall hurry to stretch out her hands to God.
\par }{\Q \VS{32}Sing to God, you kingdoms of the earth!
\par }{\QB Sing praises to the Lord!
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{33}To him who rides on the heaven of heavens, which are of old;
\par }{\QB behold, he utters his voice, a mighty voice.
\par }{\Q \VS{34}Ascribe strength to God!
\par }{\QB His excellency is over Israel,
\par }{\QB his strength is in the skies.
\par }{\Q \VS{35}You are awesome, God, in your sanctuaries.
\par }{\QB The God of Israel gives strength and power to his people.
\par }{\QB Praise be to God!

\par }\PsalmChap{69}{\D For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Lilies.” By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Save me, God,
\par }{\QB for the waters have come up to my neck!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I sink in deep mire, where there is no foothold.
\par }{\QB I have come into deep waters, where the floods overflow me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}I am weary with my crying.
\par }{\QB My throat is dry.
\par }{\QB My eyes fail looking for my God.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Those who hate me without a cause are more than the hairs of my head.
\par }{\QB Those who want to cut me off, being my enemies wrongfully, are mighty.
\par }{\QB I have to restore what I didn’t take away.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}God, you know my foolishness.
\par }{\QB My sins aren’t hidden from you.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Don’t let those who wait for you be shamed through me, Lord Yahweh of Armies.
\par }{\QB Don’t let those who seek you be brought to dishonor through me, God of Israel.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Because for your sake, I have borne reproach.
\par }{\QB Shame has covered my face.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}I have become a stranger to my brothers,
\par }{\QB an alien to my mother’s children.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}For the zeal of your house consumes me.
\par }{\QB The reproaches of those who reproach you have fallen on me.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}When I wept and I fasted,
\par }{\QB that was to my reproach.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}When I made sackcloth my clothing,
\par }{\QB I became a byword to them.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Those who sit in the gate talk about me.
\par }{\QB I am the song of the drunkards.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}But as for me, my prayer is to you, Yahweh, in an acceptable time.
\par }{\QB God, in the abundance of your loving kindness, answer me in the truth of your salvation.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Deliver me out of the mire, and don’t let me sink.
\par }{\QB Let me be delivered from those who hate me, and out of the deep waters.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Don’t let the flood waters overwhelm me,
\par }{\QB neither let the deep swallow me up.
\par }{\QB Don’t let the pit shut its mouth on me.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Answer me, Yahweh, for your loving kindness is good.
\par }{\QB According to the multitude of your tender mercies, turn to me.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Don’t hide your face from your servant,
\par }{\QB for I am in distress.
\par }{\QB Answer me speedily!
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Draw near to my soul and redeem it.
\par }{\QB Ransom me because of my enemies.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}You know my reproach, my shame, and my dishonor.
\par }{\QB My adversaries are all before you.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Reproach has broken my heart, and I am full of heaviness.
\par }{\QB I looked for some to take pity, but there was none;
\par }{\QB for comforters, but I found none.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}They also gave me poison for my food.
\par }{\QB In my thirst, they gave me vinegar to drink.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}Let their table before them become a snare.
\par }{\QB May it become a retribution and a trap.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Let their eyes be darkened, so that they can’t see.
\par }{\QB Let their backs be continually bent.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}Pour out your indignation on them.
\par }{\QB Let the fierceness of your anger overtake them.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}Let their habitation be desolate.
\par }{\QB Let no one dwell in their tents.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}For they persecute him whom you have wounded.
\par }{\QB They tell of the sorrow of those whom you have hurt.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}Charge them with crime upon crime.
\par }{\QB Don’t let them come into your righteousness.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}Let them be blotted out of the book of life,
\par }{\QB and not be written with the righteous.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}But I am in pain and distress.
\par }{\QB Let your salvation, God, protect me.
\par }{\Q \VS{30}I will praise the name of God with a song,
\par }{\QB and will magnify him with thanksgiving.
\par }{\Q \VS{31}It will please Yahweh better than an ox,
\par }{\QB or a bull that has horns and hoofs.
\par }{\Q \VS{32}The humble have seen it, and are glad.
\par }{\QB You who seek after God, let your heart live.
\par }{\Q \VS{33}For Yahweh hears the needy,
\par }{\QB and doesn’t despise his captive people.
\par }{\Q \VS{34}Let heaven and earth praise him;
\par }{\QB the seas, and everything that moves therein!
\par }{\Q \VS{35}For God will save Zion, and build the cities of Judah.
\par }{\QB They shall settle there, and own it.
\par }{\Q \VS{36}The children also of his servants shall inherit it.
\par }{\QB Those who love his name shall dwell therein.

\par }\PsalmChap{70}{\D For the Chief Musician. By David. A reminder.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Hurry, God, to deliver me.
\par }{\QB Come quickly to help me, Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Let them be disappointed and confounded who seek my soul.
\par }{\QB Let those who desire my ruin be turned back in disgrace.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Let them be turned because of their shame
\par }{\QB who say, “Aha! Aha!”
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Let all those who seek you rejoice and be glad in you.
\par }{\QB Let those who love your salvation continually say,
\par }{\QB “Let God be exalted!”
\par }{\Q \VS{5}But I am poor and needy.
\par }{\QB Come to me quickly, God.
\par }{\Q You are my help and my deliverer.
\par }{\QB Yahweh, don’t delay.
\par }{\BB \par }
\PsalmChap{71}{\Q \VerseOne{1}In you, Yahweh, I take refuge.
\par }{\QB Never let me be disappointed.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Deliver me in your righteousness, and rescue me.
\par }{\QB Turn your ear to me, and save me.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Be to me a rock of refuge to which I may always go.
\par }{\QB Give the command to save me,
\par }{\QB for you are my rock and my fortress.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Rescue me, my God, from the hand of the wicked,
\par }{\QB from the hand of the unrighteous and cruel man.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}For you are my hope, Lord Yahweh,
\par }{\QB my confidence from my youth.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I have relied on you from the womb.
\par }{\QB You are he who took me out of my mother’s womb.
\par }{\QB I will always praise you.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}I am a marvel to many,
\par }{\QB but you are my strong refuge.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}My mouth shall be filled with your praise,
\par }{\QB with your honor all day long.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Don’t reject me in my old age.
\par }{\QB Don’t forsake me when my strength fails.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}For my enemies talk about me.
\par }{\QB Those who watch for my soul conspire together,
\par }{\QB \VS{11}saying, “God has forsaken him.
\par }{\QB Pursue and take him, for no one will rescue him.”
\par }{\Q \VS{12}God, don’t be far from me.
\par }{\QB My God, hurry to help me.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Let my accusers be disappointed and consumed.
\par }{\QB Let them be covered with disgrace and scorn who want to harm me.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}But I will always hope,
\par }{\QB and will add to all of your praise.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}My mouth will tell about your righteousness,
\par }{\QB and of your salvation all day,
\par }{\QB though I don’t know its full measure.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}I will come with the mighty acts of the Lord Yahweh.
\par }{\QB I will make mention of your righteousness, even of yours alone.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}God, you have taught me from my youth.
\par }{\QB Until now, I have declared your wondrous works.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Yes, even when I am old and gray-haired, God, don’t forsake me,
\par }{\QB until I have declared your strength to the next generation,
\par }{\QB your might to everyone who is to come.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Your righteousness also, God, reaches to the heavens;
\par }{\QB you have done great things.
\par }{\QB God, who is like you?
\par }{\Q \VS{20}You, who have shown us many and bitter troubles,
\par }{\QB you will let me live.
\par }{\QB You will bring us up again from the depths of the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Increase my honor
\par }{\QB and comfort me again.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}I will also praise you with the harp for your faithfulness, my God.
\par }{\QB I sing praises to you with the lyre, Holy One of Israel.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}My lips shall shout for joy!
\par }{\QB My soul, which you have redeemed, sings praises to you!
\par }{\Q \VS{24}My tongue will also talk about your righteousness all day long,
\par }{\QB for they are disappointed, and they are confounded,
\par }{\QB who want to harm me.

\par }\PsalmChap{72}{\D By Solomon.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}God, give the king your justice;
\par }{\QB your righteousness to the royal son.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}He will judge your people with righteousness,
\par }{\QB and your poor with justice.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}The mountains shall bring prosperity to the people.
\par }{\QB The hills bring the fruit of righteousness.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}He will judge the poor of the people.
\par }{\QB He will save the children of the needy,
\par }{\QB and will break the oppressor in pieces.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They shall fear you while the sun endures;
\par }{\QB and as long as the moon, throughout all generations.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}He will come down like rain on the mown grass,
\par }{\QB as showers that water the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}In his days, the righteous shall flourish,
\par }{\QB and abundance of peace, until the moon is no more.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}He shall have dominion also from sea to sea,
\par }{\QB from the River to the ends of the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Those who dwell in the wilderness shall bow before him.
\par }{\QB His enemies shall lick the dust.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}The kings of Tarshish and of the islands will bring tribute.
\par }{\QB The kings of Sheba and Seba shall offer gifts.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Yes, all kings shall fall down before him.
\par }{\QB All nations shall serve him.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}For he will deliver the needy when he cries;
\par }{\QB the poor, who has no helper.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}He will have pity on the poor and needy.
\par }{\QB He will save the souls of the needy.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}He will redeem their soul from oppression and violence.
\par }{\QB Their blood will be precious in his sight.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}They shall live, and to him shall be given of the gold of Sheba.
\par }{\QB Men shall pray for him continually.
\par }{\QB They shall bless him all day long.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Abundance of grain shall be throughout the land.
\par }{\QB Its fruit sways like Lebanon.
\par }{\QB Let it flourish, thriving like the grass of the field.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}His name endures forever.
\par }{\QB His name continues as long as the sun.
\par }{\Q Men shall be blessed by him.
\par }{\QB All nations will call him blessed.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{18}Praise be to Yahweh God, the God of Israel,
\par }{\QB who alone does marvelous deeds.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Blessed be his glorious name forever!
\par }{\QB Let the whole earth be filled with his glory!
\par }{\Q Amen and amen.
\par }{\BB \par }{\PP \VS{20}This ends the prayers by David, the son of Jesse.

\par }{\MS BOOK 3
\par }\PsalmChap{73}{\D A Psalm by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Surely God\FTNT{*}{{\FR 73:1 }
The Hebrew word rendered “God” is “אֱלֹהִ֑ים” (Elohim).} is good to Israel,
\par }{\QB to those who are pure in heart.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}But as for me, my feet were almost gone.
\par }{\QB My steps had nearly slipped.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For I was envious of the arrogant,
\par }{\QB when I saw the prosperity of the wicked.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For there are no struggles in their death,
\par }{\QB but their strength is firm.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They are free from burdens of men,
\par }{\QB neither are they plagued like other men.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Therefore pride is like a chain around their neck.
\par }{\QB Violence covers them like a garment.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Their eyes bulge with fat.
\par }{\QB Their minds pass the limits of conceit.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}They scoff and speak with malice.
\par }{\QB In arrogance, they threaten oppression.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}They have set their mouth in the heavens.
\par }{\QB Their tongue walks through the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Therefore their people return to them,
\par }{\QB and they drink up waters of abundance.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}They say, “How does God know?
\par }{\QB Is there knowledge in the Most High?”
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Behold, these are the wicked.
\par }{\QB Being always at ease, they increase in riches.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Surely I have cleansed my heart in vain,
\par }{\QB and washed my hands in innocence,
\par }{\Q \VS{14}For all day long I have been plagued,
\par }{\QB and punished every morning.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}If I had said, “I will speak thus”;
\par }{\QB behold, I would have betrayed the generation of your children.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}When I tried to understand this,
\par }{\QB it was too painful for me,
\par }{\Q \VS{17}until I entered God’s sanctuary,
\par }{\QB and considered their latter end.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Surely you set them in slippery places.
\par }{\QB You throw them down to destruction.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}How they are suddenly destroyed!
\par }{\QB They are completely swept away with terrors.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}As a dream when one wakes up,
\par }{\QB so, Lord,\FTNT{†}{{\FR 73:20 }
The word translated “Lord” is “Adonai.”} when you awake, you will despise their fantasies.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}For my soul was grieved.
\par }{\QB I was embittered in my heart.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}I was so senseless and ignorant.
\par }{\QB I was a brute beast before you.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Nevertheless, I am continually with you.
\par }{\QB You have held my right hand.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}You will guide me with your counsel,
\par }{\QB and afterward receive me to glory.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}Whom do I have in heaven?
\par }{\QB There is no one on earth whom I desire besides you.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}My flesh and my heart fails,
\par }{\QB but God is the strength of my heart and my portion forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}For, behold, those who are far from you shall perish.
\par }{\QB You have destroyed all those who are unfaithful to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}But it is good for me to come close to God.
\par }{\QB I have made the Lord Yahweh\FTNT{‡}{{\FR 73:28 }
“Yahweh” is God’s proper Name, sometimes rendered “LORD” (all caps) in other translations.} my refuge,
\par }{\QB that I may tell of all your works.
\par }{\BB \par }
\PsalmChap{74}{\D A contemplation by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}God, why have you rejected us forever?
\par }{\QB Why does your anger smolder against the sheep of your pasture?
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Remember your congregation, which you purchased of old,
\par }{\QB which you have redeemed to be the tribe of your inheritance:
\par }{\QB Mount Zion, in which you have lived.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Lift up your feet to the perpetual ruins,
\par }{\QB all the evil that the enemy has done in the sanctuary.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Your adversaries have roared in the middle of your assembly.
\par }{\QB They have set up their standards as signs.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They behaved like men wielding axes,
\par }{\QB cutting through a thicket of trees.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Now they break all its carved work down with hatchet and hammers.
\par }{\QB \VS{7}They have burned your sanctuary to the ground.
\par }{\QB They have profaned the dwelling place of your Name.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}They said in their heart, “We will crush them completely.”
\par }{\QB They have burned up all the places in the land where God was worshiped.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}We see no miraculous signs.
\par }{\QB There is no longer any prophet,
\par }{\QB neither is there among us anyone who knows how long.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}How long, God, shall the adversary reproach?
\par }{\QB Shall the enemy blaspheme your name forever?
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Why do you draw back your hand, even your right hand?
\par }{\QB Take it from your chest and consume them!
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{12}Yet God is my King of old,
\par }{\QB working salvation throughout the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}You divided the sea by your strength.
\par }{\QB You broke the heads of the sea monsters in the waters.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}You broke the heads of Leviathan in pieces.
\par }{\QB You gave him as food to people and desert creatures.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}You opened up spring and stream.
\par }{\QB You dried up mighty rivers.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}The day is yours, the night is also yours.
\par }{\QB You have prepared the light and the sun.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}You have set all the boundaries of the earth.
\par }{\QB You have made summer and winter.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{18}Remember this, that the enemy has mocked you, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB Foolish people have blasphemed your name.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Don’t deliver the soul of your dove to wild beasts.
\par }{\QB Don’t forget the life of your poor forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Honor your covenant,
\par }{\QB for haunts of violence fill the dark places of the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Don’t let the oppressed return ashamed.
\par }{\QB Let the poor and needy praise your name.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}Arise, God! Plead your own cause.
\par }{\QB Remember how the foolish man mocks you all day.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Don’t forget the voice of your adversaries.
\par }{\QB The tumult of those who rise up against you ascends continually.
\par }{\BB \par }
\PsalmChap{75}{\D For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “Do Not Destroy.” A Psalm by Asaph. A song.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}We give thanks to you, God.
\par }{\QB We give thanks, for your Name is near.
\par }{\QB Men tell about your wondrous works.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{2}When I choose the appointed time,
\par }{\QB I will judge blamelessly.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}The earth and all its inhabitants quake.
\par }{\QB I firmly hold its pillars.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{4}I said to the arrogant, “Don’t boast!”
\par }{\QB I said to the wicked, “Don’t lift up the horn.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Don’t lift up your horn on high.
\par }{\QB Don’t speak with a stiff neck.”
\par }{\Q \VS{6}For neither from the east, nor from the west,
\par }{\QB nor yet from the south, comes exaltation.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}But God is the judge.
\par }{\QB He puts down one, and lifts up another.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}For in Yahweh’s hand there is a cup,
\par }{\QB full of foaming wine mixed with spices.
\par }{\Q He pours it out.
\par }{\QB Indeed the wicked of the earth drink and drink it to its very dregs.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{9}But I will declare this forever:
\par }{\QB I will sing praises to the God of Jacob.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}I will cut off all the horns of the wicked,
\par }{\QB but the horns of the righteous shall be lifted up.
\par }{\BB \par }
\PsalmChap{76}{\D For the Chief Musician. On stringed instruments. A Psalm by Asaph. A song.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}In Judah, God is known.
\par }{\QB His name is great in Israel.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}His tabernacle is also in Salem;
\par }{\QB His dwelling place in Zion.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}There he broke the flaming arrows of the bow,
\par }{\QB the shield, and the sword, and the weapons of war.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{4}Glorious are you, and excellent,
\par }{\QB more than mountains of game.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Valiant men lie plundered,
\par }{\QB they have slept their last sleep.
\par }{\QB None of the men of war can lift their hands.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}At your rebuke, God of Jacob,
\par }{\QB both chariot and horse are cast into a dead sleep.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}You, even you, are to be feared.
\par }{\QB Who can stand in your sight when you are angry?
\par }{\Q \VS{8}You pronounced judgment from heaven.
\par }{\QB The earth feared, and was silent,
\par }{\QB \VS{9}when God arose to judgment,
\par }{\QB to save all the afflicted ones of the earth.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{10}Surely the wrath of man praises you.
\par }{\QB The survivors of your wrath are restrained.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Make vows to Yahweh your God, and fulfill them!
\par }{\QB Let all of his neighbors bring presents to him who is to be feared.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}He will cut off the spirit of princes.
\par }{\QB He is feared by the kings of the earth.
