\PsalmChap{77}{\D For the Chief Musician. To Jeduthun. A Psalm by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}My cry goes to God!
\par }{\QB Indeed, I cry to God for help,
\par }{\QB and for him to listen to me.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}In the day of my trouble I sought the Lord.
\par }{\QB My hand was stretched out in the night, and didn’t get tired.
\par }{\QB My soul refused to be comforted.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}I remember God, and I groan.
\par }{\QB I complain, and my spirit is overwhelmed.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{4}You hold my eyelids open.
\par }{\QB I am so troubled that I can’t speak.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}I have considered the days of old,
\par }{\QB the years of ancient times.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I remember my song in the night.
\par }{\QB I consider in my own heart;
\par }{\QB my spirit diligently inquires:
\par }{\Q \VS{7}“Will the Lord reject us forever?
\par }{\QB Will he be favorable no more?
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Has his loving kindness vanished forever?
\par }{\QB Does his promise fail for generations?
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Has God forgotten to be gracious?
\par }{\QB Has he, in anger, withheld his compassion?”
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{10}Then I thought, “I will appeal to this:
\par }{\QB the years of the right hand of the Most High.”
\par }{\Q \VS{11}I will remember Yah’s deeds;
\par }{\QB for I will remember your wonders of old.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}I will also meditate on all your work,
\par }{\QB and consider your doings.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Your way, God, is in the sanctuary.
\par }{\QB What god is great like God?
\par }{\Q \VS{14}You are the God who does wonders.
\par }{\QB You have made your strength known among the peoples.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}You have redeemed your people with your arm,
\par }{\QB the sons of Jacob and Joseph.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{16}The waters saw you, God.
\par }{\QB The waters saw you, and they writhed.
\par }{\QB The depths also convulsed.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}The clouds poured out water.
\par }{\QB The skies resounded with thunder.
\par }{\QB Your arrows also flashed around.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}The voice of your thunder was in the whirlwind.
\par }{\QB The lightnings lit up the world.
\par }{\QB The earth trembled and shook.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Your way was through the sea;
\par }{\QB your paths through the great waters.
\par }{\QB Your footsteps were not known.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}You led your people like a flock,
\par }{\QB by the hand of Moses and Aaron.
\par }{\BB \par }
\PsalmChap{78}{\D A contemplation by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Hear my teaching, my people.
\par }{\QB Turn your ears to the words of my mouth.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I will open my mouth in a parable.
\par }{\QB I will utter dark sayings of old,
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Which we have heard and known,
\par }{\QB and our fathers have told us.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}We will not hide them from their children,
\par }{\QB telling to the generation to come the praises of Yahweh,
\par }{\QB his strength, and his wondrous deeds that he has done.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}For he established a covenant in Jacob,
\par }{\QB and appointed a teaching in Israel,
\par }{\QB which he commanded our fathers,
\par }{\QB that they should make them known to their children;
\par }{\Q \VS{6}that the generation to come might know, even the children who should be born;
\par }{\QB who should arise and tell their children,
\par }{\Q \VS{7}that they might set their hope in God,
\par }{\QB and not forget God’s deeds,
\par }{\QB but keep his commandments,
\par }{\Q \VS{8}and might not be as their fathers,
\par }{\QB a stubborn and rebellious generation,
\par }{\QB a generation that didn’t make their hearts loyal,
\par }{\QB whose spirit was not steadfast with God.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}The children of Ephraim, being armed and carrying bows,
\par }{\QB turned back in the day of battle.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}They didn’t keep God’s covenant,
\par }{\QB and refused to walk in his law.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}They forgot his doings,
\par }{\QB his wondrous deeds that he had shown them.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}He did marvelous things in the sight of their fathers,
\par }{\QB in the land of Egypt, in the field of Zoan.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}He split the sea, and caused them to pass through.
\par }{\QB He made the waters stand as a heap.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}In the daytime he also led them with a cloud,
\par }{\QB and all night with a light of fire.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}He split rocks in the wilderness,
\par }{\QB and gave them drink abundantly as out of the depths.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}He brought streams also out of the rock,
\par }{\QB and caused waters to run down like rivers.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Yet they still went on to sin against him,
\par }{\QB to rebel against the Most High in the desert.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}They tempted God in their heart
\par }{\QB by asking food according to their desire.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Yes, they spoke against God.
\par }{\QB They said, “Can God prepare a table in the wilderness?
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Behold, he struck the rock, so that waters gushed out,
\par }{\QB and streams overflowed.
\par }{\Q Can he give bread also?
\par }{\QB Will he provide meat for his people?”
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Therefore Yahweh heard, and was angry.
\par }{\QB A fire was kindled against Jacob,
\par }{\QB anger also went up against Israel,
\par }{\Q \VS{22}because they didn’t believe in God,
\par }{\QB and didn’t trust in his salvation.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Yet he commanded the skies above,
\par }{\QB and opened the doors of heaven.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}He rained down manna on them to eat,
\par }{\QB and gave them food from the sky.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}Man ate the bread of angels.
\par }{\QB He sent them food to the full.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}He caused the east wind to blow in the sky.
\par }{\QB By his power he guided the south wind.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}He also rained meat on them as the dust,
\par }{\QB winged birds as the sand of the seas.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}He let them fall in the middle of their camp,
\par }{\QB around their habitations.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}So they ate, and were well filled.
\par }{\QB He gave them their own desire.
\par }{\Q \VS{30}They didn’t turn from their cravings.
\par }{\QB Their food was yet in their mouths,
\par }{\QB \VS{31}when the anger of God went up against them,
\par }{\QB killed some of their fattest,
\par }{\QB and struck down the young men of Israel.
\par }{\Q \VS{32}For all this they still sinned,
\par }{\QB and didn’t believe in his wondrous works.
\par }{\Q \VS{33}Therefore he consumed their days in vanity,
\par }{\QB and their years in terror.
\par }{\Q \VS{34}When he killed them, then they inquired after him.
\par }{\QB They returned and sought God earnestly.
\par }{\Q \VS{35}They remembered that God was their rock,
\par }{\QB the Most High God, their redeemer.
\par }{\Q \VS{36}But they flattered him with their mouth,
\par }{\QB and lied to him with their tongue.
\par }{\Q \VS{37}For their heart was not right with him,
\par }{\QB neither were they faithful in his covenant.
\par }{\Q \VS{38}But he, being merciful, forgave iniquity, and didn’t destroy them.
\par }{\QB Yes, many times he turned his anger away,
\par }{\QB and didn’t stir up all his wrath.
\par }{\Q \VS{39}He remembered that they were but flesh,
\par }{\QB a wind that passes away, and doesn’t come again.
\par }{\Q \VS{40}How often they rebelled against him in the wilderness,
\par }{\QB and grieved him in the desert!
\par }{\Q \VS{41}They turned again and tempted God,
\par }{\QB and provoked the Holy One of Israel.
\par }{\Q \VS{42}They didn’t remember his hand,
\par }{\QB nor the day when he redeemed them from the adversary;
\par }{\Q \VS{43}how he set his signs in Egypt,
\par }{\QB his wonders in the field of Zoan,
\par }{\Q \VS{44}he turned their rivers into blood,
\par }{\QB and their streams, so that they could not drink.
\par }{\Q \VS{45}He sent among them swarms of flies, which devoured them;
\par }{\QB and frogs, which destroyed them.
\par }{\Q \VS{46}He gave also their increase to the caterpillar,
\par }{\QB and their labor to the locust.
\par }{\Q \VS{47}He destroyed their vines with hail,
\par }{\QB their sycamore fig trees with frost.
\par }{\Q \VS{48}He gave over their livestock also to the hail,
\par }{\QB and their flocks to hot thunderbolts.
\par }{\Q \VS{49}He threw on them the fierceness of his anger,
\par }{\QB wrath, indignation, and trouble,
\par }{\QB and a band of angels of evil.
\par }{\Q \VS{50}He made a path for his anger.
\par }{\QB He didn’t spare their soul from death,
\par }{\QB but gave their life over to the pestilence,
\par }{\Q \VS{51}and struck all the firstborn in Egypt,
\par }{\QB the chief of their strength in the tents of Ham.
\par }{\Q \VS{52}But he led out his own people like sheep,
\par }{\QB and guided them in the wilderness like a flock.
\par }{\Q \VS{53}He led them safely, so that they weren’t afraid,
\par }{\QB but the sea overwhelmed their enemies.
\par }{\Q \VS{54}He brought them to the border of his sanctuary,
\par }{\QB to this mountain, which his right hand had taken.
\par }{\Q \VS{55}He also drove out the nations before them,
\par }{\QB allotted them for an inheritance by line,
\par }{\QB and made the tribes of Israel to dwell in their tents.
\par }{\Q \VS{56}Yet they tempted and rebelled against the Most High God,
\par }{\QB and didn’t keep his testimonies,
\par }{\Q \VS{57}but turned back, and dealt treacherously like their fathers.
\par }{\QB They were twisted like a deceitful bow.
\par }{\Q \VS{58}For they provoked him to anger with their high places,
\par }{\QB and moved him to jealousy with their engraved images.
\par }{\Q \VS{59}When God heard this, he was angry,
\par }{\QB and greatly abhorred Israel,
\par }{\Q \VS{60}so that he abandoned the tent of Shiloh,
\par }{\QB the tent which he placed among men,
\par }{\Q \VS{61}and delivered his strength into captivity,
\par }{\QB his glory into the adversary’s hand.
\par }{\Q \VS{62}He also gave his people over to the sword,
\par }{\QB and was angry with his inheritance.
\par }{\Q \VS{63}Fire devoured their young men.
\par }{\QB Their virgins had no wedding song.
\par }{\Q \VS{64}Their priests fell by the sword,
\par }{\QB and their widows couldn’t weep.
\par }{\Q \VS{65}Then the Lord awakened as one out of sleep,
\par }{\QB like a mighty man who shouts by reason of wine.
\par }{\Q \VS{66}He struck his adversaries backward.
\par }{\QB He put them to a perpetual reproach.
\par }{\Q \VS{67}Moreover he rejected the tent of Joseph,
\par }{\QB and didn’t choose the tribe of Ephraim,
\par }{\Q \VS{68}But chose the tribe of Judah,
\par }{\QB Mount Zion which he loved.
\par }{\Q \VS{69}He built his sanctuary like the heights,
\par }{\QB like the earth which he has established forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{70}He also chose David his servant,
\par }{\QB and took him from the sheepfolds;
\par }{\Q \VS{71}from following the ewes that have their young,
\par }{\QB he brought him to be the shepherd of Jacob, his people,
\par }{\QB and Israel, his inheritance.
\par }{\Q \VS{72}So he was their shepherd according to the integrity of his heart,
\par }{\QB and guided them by the skillfulness of his hands.
\par }{\BB \par }
\PsalmChap{79}{\D A Psalm by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}God, the nations have come into your inheritance.
\par }{\QB They have defiled your holy temple.
\par }{\QB They have laid Jerusalem in heaps.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}They have given the dead bodies of your servants to be food for the birds of the sky,
\par }{\QB the flesh of your saints to the animals of the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}They have shed their blood like water around Jerusalem.
\par }{\QB There was no one to bury them.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}We have become a reproach to our neighbors,
\par }{\QB a scoffing and derision to those who are around us.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}How long, Yahweh?
\par }{\QB Will you be angry forever?
\par }{\QB Will your jealousy burn like fire?
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Pour out your wrath on the nations that don’t know you,
\par }{\QB on the kingdoms that don’t call on your name;
\par }{\Q \VS{7}for they have devoured Jacob,
\par }{\QB and destroyed his homeland.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Don’t hold the iniquities of our forefathers against us.
\par }{\QB Let your tender mercies speedily meet us,
\par }{\QB for we are in desperate need.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Help us, God of our salvation, for the glory of your name.
\par }{\QB Deliver us, and forgive our sins, for your name’s sake.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Why should the nations say, “Where is their God?”
\par }{\QB Let it be known among the nations, before our eyes,
\par }{\QB that vengeance for your servants’ blood is being poured out.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Let the sighing of the prisoner come before you.
\par }{\QB According to the greatness of your power, preserve those who are sentenced to death.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Pay back to our neighbors seven times into their bosom
\par }{\QB their reproach with which they have reproached you, Lord.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}So we, your people and sheep of your pasture,
\par }{\QB will give you thanks forever.
\par }{\QB We will praise you forever, to all generations.
\par }{\BB \par }
\PsalmChap{80}{\D For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “The Lilies of the Covenant.” A Psalm by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Hear us, Shepherd of Israel,
\par }{\QB you who lead Joseph like a flock,
\par }{\QB you who sit above the cherubim, shine out.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Before Ephraim and Benjamin and Manasseh, stir up your might!
\par }{\QB Come to save us!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Turn us again, God.
\par }{\QB Cause your face to shine,
\par }{\QB and we will be saved.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{4}Yahweh God of Armies,
\par }{\QB how long will you be angry against the prayer of your people?
\par }{\Q \VS{5}You have fed them with the bread of tears,
\par }{\QB and given them tears to drink in large measure.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}You make us a source of contention to our neighbors.
\par }{\QB Our enemies laugh among themselves.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Turn us again, God of Armies.
\par }{\QB Cause your face to shine,
\par }{\QB and we will be saved.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{8}You brought a vine out of Egypt.
\par }{\QB You drove out the nations, and planted it.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}You cleared the ground for it.
\par }{\QB It took deep root, and filled the land.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}The mountains were covered with its shadow.
\par }{\QB Its boughs were like God’s cedars.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}It sent out its branches to the sea,
\par }{\QB its shoots to the River.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Why have you broken down its walls,
\par }{\QB so that all those who pass by the way pluck it?
\par }{\Q \VS{13}The boar out of the wood ravages it.
\par }{\QB The wild animals of the field feed on it.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Turn again, we beg you, God of Armies.
\par }{\QB Look down from heaven, and see, and visit this vine,
\par }{\Q \VS{15}the stock which your right hand planted,
\par }{\QB the branch that you made strong for yourself.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}It’s burned with fire.
\par }{\QB It’s cut down.
\par }{\QB They perish at your rebuke.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Let your hand be on the man of your right hand,
\par }{\QB on the son of man whom you made strong for yourself.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}So we will not turn away from you.
\par }{\QB Revive us, and we will call on your name.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Turn us again, Yahweh God of Armies.
\par }{\QB Cause your face to shine, and we will be saved.

\par }\PsalmChap{81}{\D For the Chief Musician. On an instrument of Gath. By Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Sing aloud to God, our strength!
\par }{\QB Make a joyful shout to the God of Jacob!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Raise a song, and bring here the tambourine,
\par }{\QB the pleasant lyre with the harp.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Blow the trumpet at the New Moon,
\par }{\QB at the full moon, on our feast day.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For it is a statute for Israel,
\par }{\QB an ordinance of the God of Jacob.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}He appointed it in Joseph for a covenant,
\par }{\QB when he went out over the land of Egypt,
\par }{\QB I heard a language that I didn’t know.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}“I removed his shoulder from the burden.
\par }{\QB His hands were freed from the basket.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}You called in trouble, and I delivered you.
\par }{\QB I answered you in the secret place of thunder.
\par }{\QB I tested you at the waters of Meribah.”
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{8}“Hear, my people, and I will testify to you,
\par }{\QB Israel, if you would listen to me!
\par }{\Q \VS{9}There shall be no strange god in you,
\par }{\QB neither shall you worship any foreign god.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}I am Yahweh, your God,
\par }{\QB who brought you up out of the land of Egypt.
\par }{\QB Open your mouth wide, and I will fill it.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}But my people didn’t listen to my voice.
\par }{\QB Israel desired none of me.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}So I let them go after the stubbornness of their hearts,
\par }{\QB that they might walk in their own counsels.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Oh that my people would listen to me,
\par }{\QB that Israel would walk in my ways!
\par }{\Q \VS{14}I would soon subdue their enemies,
\par }{\QB and turn my hand against their adversaries.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}The haters of Yahweh would cringe before him,
\par }{\QB and their punishment would last forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}But he would have also fed them with the finest of the wheat.
\par }{\QB I will satisfy you with honey out of the rock.”

\par }\PsalmChap{82}{\D A Psalm by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}God presides in the great assembly.
\par }{\QB He judges among the gods.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}“How long will you judge unjustly,
\par }{\QB and show partiality to the wicked?”
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{3}“Defend the weak, the poor, and the fatherless.
\par }{\QB Maintain the rights of the poor and oppressed.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Rescue the weak and needy.
\par }{\QB Deliver them out of the hand of the wicked.”
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They don’t know, neither do they understand.
\par }{\QB They walk back and forth in darkness.
\par }{\QB All the foundations of the earth are shaken.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I said, “You are gods,
\par }{\QB all of you are sons of the Most High.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Nevertheless you shall die like men,
\par }{\QB and fall like one of the rulers.”
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Arise, God, judge the earth,
\par }{\QB for you inherit all of the nations.

\par }\PsalmChap{83}{\D A song. A Psalm by Asaph.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}God, don’t keep silent.
\par }{\QB Don’t keep silent,
\par }{\QB and don’t be still, God.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}For, behold, your enemies are stirred up.
\par }{\QB Those who hate you have lifted up their heads.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}They conspire with cunning against your people.
\par }{\QB They plot against your cherished ones.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}“Come,” they say, “let’s destroy them as a nation,
\par }{\QB that the name of Israel may be remembered no more.”
\par }{\Q \VS{5}For they have conspired together with one mind.
\par }{\QB They form an alliance against you.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}The tents of Edom and the Ishmaelites;
\par }{\QB Moab, and the Hagrites;
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Gebal, Ammon, and Amalek;
\par }{\QB Philistia with the inhabitants of Tyre;
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Assyria also is joined with them.
\par }{\QB They have helped the children of Lot.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{9}Do to them as you did to Midian,
\par }{\QB as to Sisera, as to Jabin, at the river Kishon;
\par }{\Q \VS{10}who perished at Endor,
\par }{\QB who became as dung for the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Make their nobles like Oreb and Zeeb,
\par }{\QB yes, all their princes like Zebah and Zalmunna,
\par }{\QB \VS{12}who said, “Let’s take possession of God’s pasture lands.”
\par }{\Q \VS{13}My God, make them like tumbleweed,
\par }{\QB like chaff before the wind.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}As the fire that burns the forest,
\par }{\QB as the flame that sets the mountains on fire,
\par }{\QB \VS{15}so pursue them with your tempest,
\par }{\QB and terrify them with your storm.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Fill their faces with confusion,
\par }{\QB that they may seek your name, Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Let them be disappointed and dismayed forever.
\par }{\QB Yes, let them be confounded and perish;
\par }{\Q \VS{18}that they may know that you alone, whose name is Yahweh,
\par }{\QB are the Most High over all the earth.

\par }\PsalmChap{84}{\D For the Chief Musician. On an instrument of Gath. A Psalm by the sons of Korah.

\par }{\Q \VS{2}My soul longs, and even faints for the courts of Yahweh.
\par }{\QB My heart and my flesh cry out for the living God.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Yes, the sparrow has found a home,
\par }{\QB and the swallow a nest for herself, where she may have her young,
\par }{\QB near your altars, Yahweh of Armies, my King, and my God.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Blessed are those who dwell in your house.
\par }{\QB They are always praising you.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{5}Blessed are those whose strength is in you,
\par }{\QB who have set their hearts on a pilgrimage.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Passing through the valley of Weeping, they make it a place of springs.
\par }{\QB Yes, the autumn rain covers it with blessings.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}They go from strength to strength.
\par }{\QB Every one of them appears before God in Zion.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Yahweh, God of Armies, hear my prayer.
\par }{\QB Listen, God of Jacob.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{9}Behold, God our shield,
\par }{\QB look at the face of your anointed.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}For a day in your courts is better than a thousand.
\par }{\QB I would rather be a doorkeeper in the house of my God,
\par }{\QB than to dwell in the tents of wickedness.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}For Yahweh God is a sun and a shield.
\par }{\QB Yahweh will give grace and glory.
\par }{\QB He withholds no good thing from those who walk blamelessly.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Yahweh of Armies,
\par }{\QB blessed is the man who trusts in you.

\par }\PsalmChap{86}{\D A Prayer by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Hear, Yahweh, and answer me,
\par }{\QB for I am poor and needy.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Preserve my soul, for I am godly.
\par }{\QB You, my God, save your servant who trusts in you.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Be merciful to me, Lord,
\par }{\QB for I call to you all day long.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Bring joy to the soul of your servant,
\par }{\QB for to you, Lord, do I lift up my soul.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}For you, Lord, are good, and ready to forgive,
\par }{\QB abundant in loving kindness to all those who call on you.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Hear, Yahweh, my prayer.
\par }{\QB Listen to the voice of my petitions.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}In the day of my trouble I will call on you,
\par }{\QB for you will answer me.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}There is no one like you among the gods, Lord,
\par }{\QB nor any deeds like your deeds.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}All nations you have made will come and worship before you, Lord.
\par }{\QB They shall glorify your name.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}For you are great, and do wondrous things.
\par }{\QB You are God alone.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Teach me your way, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB I will walk in your truth.
\par }{\QB Make my heart undivided to fear your name.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}I will praise you, Lord my God, with my whole heart.
\par }{\QB I will glorify your name forever more.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}For your loving kindness is great toward me.
\par }{\QB You have delivered my soul from the lowest Sheol.\FTNT{*}{{\FR 86:13 }
Sheol is the place of the dead.}
\par }{\Q \VS{14}God, the proud have risen up against me.
\par }{\QB A company of violent men have sought after my soul,
\par }{\QB and they don’t hold regard for you before them.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}But you, Lord, are a merciful and gracious God,
\par }{\QB slow to anger, and abundant in loving kindness and truth.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Turn to me, and have mercy on me!
\par }{\QB Give your strength to your servant.
\par }{\QB Save the son of your servant.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Show me a sign of your goodness,
\par }{\QB that those who hate me may see it, and be shamed,
\par }{\QB because you, Yahweh, have helped me, and comforted me.

\par }\PsalmChap{88}{\D A Song. A Psalm by the sons of Korah. For the Chief Musician. To the tune of “The Suffering of Affliction.” A contemplation by Heman, the Ezrahite.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Yahweh, the God of my salvation,
\par }{\QB I have cried day and night before you.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Let my prayer enter into your presence.
\par }{\QB Turn your ear to my cry.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For my soul is full of troubles.
\par }{\QB My life draws near to Sheol.\FTNT{*}{{\FR 88:3 }
Sheol is the place of the dead.}
\par }{\Q \VS{4}I am counted among those who go down into the pit.
\par }{\QB I am like a man who has no help,
\par }{\QB \VS{5}set apart among the dead,
\par }{\QB like the slain who lie in the grave,
\par }{\QB whom you remember no more.
\par }{\QB They are cut off from your hand.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}You have laid me in the lowest pit,
\par }{\QB in the darkest depths.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Your wrath lies heavily on me.
\par }{\QB You have afflicted me with all your waves.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{8}You have taken my friends from me.
\par }{\QB You have made me an abomination to them.
\par }{\QB I am confined, and I can’t escape.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}My eyes are dim from grief.
\par }{\QB I have called on you daily, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB I have spread out my hands to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Do you show wonders to the dead?
\par }{\QB Do the departed spirits rise up and praise you?
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{11}Is your loving kindness declared in the grave?
\par }{\QB Or your faithfulness in Destruction?
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Are your wonders made known in the dark?
\par }{\QB Or your righteousness in the land of forgetfulness?
\par }{\Q \VS{13}But to you, Yahweh, I have cried.
\par }{\QB In the morning, my prayer comes before you.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Yahweh, why do you reject my soul?
\par }{\QB Why do you hide your face from me?
\par }{\Q \VS{15}I am afflicted and ready to die from my youth up.
\par }{\QB While I suffer your terrors, I am distracted.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Your fierce wrath has gone over me.
\par }{\QB Your terrors have cut me off.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}They came around me like water all day long.
\par }{\QB They completely engulfed me.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}You have put lover and friend far from me,
\par }{\QB and my friends into darkness.

\par }\PsalmChap{89}{\D A contemplation by Ethan, the Ezrahite.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}I will sing of the loving kindness of Yahweh forever.
\par }{\QB With my mouth, I will make known your faithfulness to all generations.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I indeed declare, “Love stands firm forever.
\par }{\QB You established the heavens.
\par }{\QB Your faithfulness is in them.”
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{3}“I have made a covenant with my chosen one,
\par }{\QB I have sworn to David, my servant,
\par }{\Q \VS{4}‘I will establish your offspring forever,
\par }{\QB and build up your throne to all generations.’ ”
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{5}The heavens will praise your wonders, Yahweh,
\par }{\QB your faithfulness also in the assembly of the holy ones.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}For who in the skies can be compared to Yahweh?
\par }{\QB Who among the sons of the heavenly beings is like Yahweh,
\par }{\Q \VS{7}a very awesome God in the council of the holy ones,
\par }{\QB to be feared above all those who are around him?
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Yahweh, God of Armies, who is a mighty one, like you?
\par }{\QB Yah, your faithfulness is around you.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}You rule the pride of the sea.
\par }{\QB When its waves rise up, you calm them.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}You have broken Rahab in pieces, like one of the slain.
\par }{\QB You have scattered your enemies with your mighty arm.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}The heavens are yours.
\par }{\QB The earth also is yours,
\par }{\QB the world and its fullness.
\par }{\QB You have founded them.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}You have created the north and the south.
\par }{\QB Tabor and Hermon rejoice in your name.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}You have a mighty arm.
\par }{\QB Your hand is strong, and your right hand is exalted.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Righteousness and justice are the foundation of your throne.
\par }{\QB Loving kindness and truth go before your face.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Blessed are the people who learn to acclaim you.
\par }{\QB They walk in the light of your presence, Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}In your name they rejoice all day.
\par }{\QB In your righteousness, they are exalted.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}For you are the glory of their strength.
\par }{\QB In your favor, our horn will be exalted.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}For our shield belongs to Yahweh,
\par }{\QB our king to the Holy One of Israel.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{19}Then you spoke in vision to your saints,
\par }{\QB and said, “I have given strength to the warrior.
\par }{\QB I have exalted a young man from the people.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}I have found David, my servant.
\par }{\QB I have anointed him with my holy oil,
\par }{\Q \VS{21}with whom my hand shall be established.
\par }{\QB My arm will also strengthen him.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}No enemy will tax him.
\par }{\QB No wicked man will oppress him.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}I will beat down his adversaries before him,
\par }{\QB and strike those who hate him.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}But my faithfulness and my loving kindness will be with him.
\par }{\QB In my name, his horn will be exalted.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}I will set his hand also on the sea,
\par }{\QB and his right hand on the rivers.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}He will call to me, ‘You are my Father,
\par }{\QB my God, and the rock of my salvation!’
\par }{\Q \VS{27}I will also appoint him my firstborn,
\par }{\QB the highest of the kings of the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}I will keep my loving kindness for him forever more.
\par }{\QB My covenant will stand firm with him.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}I will also make his offspring endure forever,
\par }{\QB and his throne as the days of heaven.
\par }{\Q \VS{30}If his children forsake my law,
\par }{\QB and don’t walk in my ordinances;
\par }{\Q \VS{31}if they break my statutes,
\par }{\QB and don’t keep my commandments;
\par }{\Q \VS{32}then I will punish their sin with the rod,
\par }{\QB and their iniquity with stripes.
\par }{\Q \VS{33}But I will not completely take my loving kindness from him,
\par }{\QB nor allow my faithfulness to fail.
\par }{\Q \VS{34}I will not break my covenant,
\par }{\QB nor alter what my lips have uttered.
\par }{\Q \VS{35}Once I have sworn by my holiness,
\par }{\QB I will not lie to David.
\par }{\Q \VS{36}His offspring will endure forever,
\par }{\QB his throne like the sun before me.
\par }{\Q \VS{37}It will be established forever like the moon,
\par }{\QB the faithful witness in the sky.”
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{38}But you have rejected and spurned.
\par }{\QB You have been angry with your anointed.
\par }{\Q \VS{39}You have renounced the covenant of your servant.
\par }{\QB You have defiled his crown in the dust.
\par }{\Q \VS{40}You have broken down all his hedges.
\par }{\QB You have brought his strongholds to ruin.
\par }{\Q \VS{41}All who pass by the way rob him.
\par }{\Q He has become a reproach to his neighbors.
\par }{\Q \VS{42}You have exalted the right hand of his adversaries.
\par }{\QB You have made all of his enemies rejoice.
\par }{\Q \VS{43}Yes, you turn back the edge of his sword,
\par }{\QB and haven’t supported him in battle.
\par }{\Q \VS{44}You have ended his splendor,
\par }{\QB and thrown his throne down to the ground.
\par }{\Q \VS{45}You have shortened the days of his youth.
\par }{\QB You have covered him with shame.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{46}How long, Yahweh?
\par }{\QB Will you hide yourself forever?
\par }{\QB Will your wrath burn like fire?
\par }{\Q \VS{47}Remember how short my time is,
\par }{\QB for what vanity you have created all the children of men!
\par }{\Q \VS{48}What man is he who shall live and not see death,
\par }{\QB who shall deliver his soul from the power of Sheol?\FTNT{*}{{\FR 89:48 }
Sheol is the place of the dead.}
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{49}Lord, where are your former loving kindnesses,
\par }{\QB which you swore to David in your faithfulness?
\par }{\Q \VS{50}Remember, Lord, the reproach of your servants,
\par }{\QB how I bear in my heart the taunts of all the mighty peoples,
\par }{\Q \VS{51}With which your enemies have mocked, Yahweh,
\par }{\QB with which they have mocked the footsteps of your anointed one.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{52}Blessed be Yahweh forever more.
\par }{\Q Amen, and Amen.

\par }\PsalmChap{90}{\D A Prayer by Moses, the man of God.\FTNT{*}{{\FR 90: }
The Hebrew word rendered “God” is “אֱלֹהִ֑ים” (Elohim).}
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Lord,\FTNT{†}{{\FR 90:1 }
The word translated “Lord” is “Adonai.”} you have been our dwelling place for all generations.
\par }{\QB \VS{2}Before the mountains were born,
\par }{\QB before you had formed the earth and the world,
\par }{\QB even from everlasting to everlasting, you are God.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}You turn man to destruction, saying,
\par }{\QB “Return, you children of men.”
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For a thousand years in your sight are just like yesterday when it is past,
\par }{\QB like a watch in the night.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}You sweep them away as they sleep.
\par }{\QB In the morning they sprout like new grass.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}In the morning it sprouts and springs up.
\par }{\QB By evening, it is withered and dry.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}For we are consumed in your anger.
\par }{\QB We are troubled in your wrath.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}You have set our iniquities before you,
\par }{\QB our secret sins in the light of your presence.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}For all our days have passed away in your wrath.
\par }{\QB We bring our years to an end as a sigh.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}The days of our years are seventy,
\par }{\QB or even by reason of strength eighty years;
\par }{\QB yet their pride is but labor and sorrow,
\par }{\QB for it passes quickly, and we fly away.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Who knows the power of your anger,
\par }{\QB your wrath according to the fear that is due to you?
\par }{\Q \VS{12}So teach us to count our days,
\par }{\QB that we may gain a heart of wisdom.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Relent, Yahweh!\FTNT{‡}{{\FR 90:13 }
“Yahweh” is God’s proper Name, sometimes rendered “LORD” (all caps) in other translations.}
\par }{\QB How long?
\par }{\QB Have compassion on your servants!
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Satisfy us in the morning with your loving kindness,
\par }{\QB that we may rejoice and be glad all our days.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Make us glad for as many days as you have afflicted us,
\par }{\QB for as many years as we have seen evil.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Let your work appear to your servants,
\par }{\QB your glory to their children.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Let the favor of the Lord our God be on us.
\par }{\QB Establish the work of our hands for us.
\par }{\QB Yes, establish the work of our hands.

\par }\PsalmChap{91}{\Q \VerseOne{1}He who dwells in the secret place of the Most High
\par }{\QB will rest in the shadow of the Almighty.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I will say of Yahweh, “He is my refuge and my fortress;
\par }{\QB my God, in whom I trust.”
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For he will deliver you from the snare of the fowler,
\par }{\QB and from the deadly pestilence.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}He will cover you with his feathers.
\par }{\QB Under his wings you will take refuge.
\par }{\QB His faithfulness is your shield and rampart.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}You shall not be afraid of the terror by night,
\par }{\QB nor of the arrow that flies by day,
\par }{\QB \VS{6}nor of the pestilence that walks in darkness,
\par }{\QB nor of the destruction that wastes at noonday.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}A thousand may fall at your side,
\par }{\QB and ten thousand at your right hand;
\par }{\QB but it will not come near you.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}You will only look with your eyes,
\par }{\QB and see the recompense of the wicked.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Because you have made Yahweh your refuge,
\par }{\QB and the Most High your dwelling place,
\par }{\Q \VS{10}no evil shall happen to you,
\par }{\QB neither shall any plague come near your dwelling.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}For he will put his angels in charge of you,
\par }{\QB to guard you in all your ways.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}They will bear you up in their hands,
\par }{\QB so that you won’t dash your foot against a stone.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}You will tread on the lion and cobra.
\par }{\QB You will trample the young lion and the serpent underfoot.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}“Because he has set his love on me, therefore I will deliver him.
\par }{\QB I will set him on high, because he has known my name.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}He will call on me, and I will answer him.
\par }{\QB I will be with him in trouble.
\par }{\QB I will deliver him, and honor him.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}I will satisfy him with long life,
\par }{\QB and show him my salvation.”

\par }\PsalmChap{92}{\D A Psalm. A song for the Sabbath day.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}It is a good thing to give thanks to Yahweh,
\par }{\QB to sing praises to your name, Most High,
\par }{\Q \VS{2}to proclaim your loving kindness in the morning,
\par }{\QB and your faithfulness every night,
\par }{\Q \VS{3}with the ten-stringed lute, with the harp,
\par }{\QB and with the melody of the lyre.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For you, Yahweh, have made me glad through your work.
\par }{\QB I will triumph in the works of your hands.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}How great are your works, Yahweh!
\par }{\QB Your thoughts are very deep.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}A senseless man doesn’t know,
\par }{\QB neither does a fool understand this:
\par }{\Q \VS{7}though the wicked spring up as the grass,
\par }{\QB and all the evildoers flourish,
\par }{\QB they will be destroyed forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}But you, Yahweh, are on high forever more.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}For, behold, your enemies, Yahweh,
\par }{\QB for, behold, your enemies shall perish.
\par }{\QB All the evildoers will be scattered.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}But you have exalted my horn like that of the wild ox.
\par }{\QB I am anointed with fresh oil.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}My eye has also seen my enemies.
\par }{\QB My ears have heard of the wicked enemies who rise up against me.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}The righteous shall flourish like the palm tree.
\par }{\QB He will grow like a cedar in Lebanon.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}They are planted in Yahweh’s house.
\par }{\QB They will flourish in our God’s courts.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}They will still produce fruit in old age.
\par }{\QB They will be full of sap and green,
\par }{\QB \VS{15}to show that Yahweh is upright.
\par }{\Q He is my rock,
\par }{\QB and there is no unrighteousness in him.

\par }\PsalmChap{101}{\D A Psalm by David.

\par }{\Q \VS{3}I will set no vile thing before my eyes.

\par }{\QB They will not cling to me.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}A perverse heart will be far from me.
\par }{\QB I will have nothing to do with evil.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}I will silence whoever secretly slanders his neighbor.
\par }{\QB I won’t tolerate one who is arrogant and conceited.

\par }{\QB he will serve me.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}He who practices deceit won’t dwell within my house.
\par }{\QB He who speaks falsehood won’t be established before my eyes.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Morning by morning, I will destroy all the wicked of the land,
\par }{\QB to cut off all the workers of iniquity from Yahweh’s city.

\par }\PsalmChap{102}{\D A Prayer of the afflicted, when he is overwhelmed and pours out his complaint before Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Hear my prayer, Yahweh!
\par }{\QB Let my cry come to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Don’t hide your face from me in the day of my distress.
\par }{\QB Turn your ear to me.
\par }{\QB Answer me quickly in the day when I call.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For my days consume away like smoke.
\par }{\QB My bones are burned as a torch.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}My heart is blighted like grass, and withered,
\par }{\QB for I forget to eat my bread.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}By reason of the voice of my groaning,
\par }{\QB my bones stick to my skin.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I am like a pelican of the wilderness.
\par }{\QB I have become as an owl of the waste places.
\par }{\QB \VS{7}I watch, and have become like a sparrow that is alone on the housetop.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}My enemies reproach me all day.
\par }{\QB Those who are mad at me use my name as a curse.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}For I have eaten ashes like bread,
\par }{\QB and mixed my drink with tears,
\par }{\QB \VS{10}because of your indignation and your wrath;
\par }{\QB for you have taken me up and thrown me away.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}My days are like a long shadow.
\par }{\QB I have withered like grass.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{12}But you, Yahweh, will remain forever;
\par }{\QB your renown endures to all generations.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}You will arise and have mercy on Zion;
\par }{\QB for it is time to have pity on her.
\par }{\QB Yes, the set time has come.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}For your servants take pleasure in her stones,
\par }{\QB and have pity on her dust.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}So the nations will fear Yahweh’s name,
\par }{\QB all the kings of the earth your glory.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}For Yahweh has built up Zion.
\par }{\QB He has appeared in his glory.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}He has responded to the prayer of the destitute,
\par }{\QB and has not despised their prayer.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}This will be written for the generation to come.
\par }{\QB A people which will be created will praise Yah.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}For he has looked down from the height of his sanctuary.
\par }{\QB From heaven, Yahweh saw the earth;
\par }{\Q \VS{20}to hear the groans of the prisoner;
\par }{\QB to free those who are condemned to death;
\par }{\Q \VS{21}that men may declare Yahweh’s name in Zion,
\par }{\QB and his praise in Jerusalem;
\par }{\Q \VS{22}when the peoples are gathered together,
\par }{\QB the kingdoms, to serve Yahweh.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{23}He weakened my strength along the course.
\par }{\QB He shortened my days.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}I said, “My God, don’t take me away in the middle of my days.
\par }{\QB Your years are throughout all generations.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}Of old, you laid the foundation of the earth.
\par }{\QB The heavens are the work of your hands.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}They will perish, but you will endure.
\par }{\QB Yes, all of them will wear out like a garment.
\par }{\QB You will change them like a cloak, and they will be changed.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}But you are the same.
\par }{\QB Your years will have no end.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}The children of your servants will continue.
\par }{\QB Their offspring will be established before you.”

\par }\PsalmChap{103}{\D By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Praise Yahweh, my soul!
\par }{\QB All that is within me, praise his holy name!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Praise Yahweh, my soul,
\par }{\QB and don’t forget all his benefits,
\par }{\Q \VS{3}who forgives all your sins,
\par }{\QB who heals all your diseases,
\par }{\Q \VS{4}who redeems your life from destruction,
\par }{\QB who crowns you with loving kindness and tender mercies,
\par }{\Q \VS{5}who satisfies your desire with good things,
\par }{\QB so that your youth is renewed like the eagle’s.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Yahweh executes righteous acts,
\par }{\QB and justice for all who are oppressed.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}He made known his ways to Moses,
\par }{\QB his deeds to the children of Israel.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Yahweh is merciful and gracious,
\par }{\QB slow to anger, and abundant in loving kindness.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}He will not always accuse;
\par }{\QB neither will he stay angry forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}He has not dealt with us according to our sins,
\par }{\QB nor repaid us for our iniquities.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}For as the heavens are high above the earth,
\par }{\QB so great is his loving kindness toward those who fear him.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}As far as the east is from the west,
\par }{\QB so far has he removed our transgressions from us.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Like a father has compassion on his children,
\par }{\QB so Yahweh has compassion on those who fear him.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}For he knows how we are made.
\par }{\QB He remembers that we are dust.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}As for man, his days are like grass.
\par }{\QB As a flower of the field, so he flourishes.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}For the wind passes over it, and it is gone.
\par }{\QB Its place remembers it no more.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}But Yahweh’s loving kindness is from everlasting to everlasting with those who fear him,
\par }{\QB his righteousness to children’s children,
\par }{\Q \VS{18}to those who keep his covenant,
\par }{\QB to those who remember to obey his precepts.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Yahweh has established his throne in the heavens.
\par }{\QB His kingdom rules over all.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Praise Yahweh, you angels of his,
\par }{\QB who are mighty in strength, who fulfill his word,
\par }{\QB obeying the voice of his word.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Praise Yahweh, all you armies of his,
\par }{\QB you servants of his, who do his pleasure.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}Praise Yahweh, all you works of his,
\par }{\QB in all places of his dominion.
\par }{\QB Praise Yahweh, my soul!

\par }\PsalmChap{104}{\Q \VerseOne{1}Bless Yahweh, my soul.
\par }{\QB Yahweh, my God, you are very great.
\par }{\QB You are clothed with honor and majesty.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}He covers himself with light as with a garment.
\par }{\QB He stretches out the heavens like a curtain.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}He lays the beams of his rooms in the waters.
\par }{\QB He makes the clouds his chariot.
\par }{\QB He walks on the wings of the wind.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}He makes his messengers\FTNT{*}{{\FR 104:4 }
or, angels} winds,
\par }{\QB and his servants flames of fire.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}He laid the foundations of the earth,
\par }{\QB that it should not be moved forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}You covered it with the deep as with a cloak.
\par }{\QB The waters stood above the mountains.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}At your rebuke they fled.
\par }{\QB At the voice of your thunder they hurried away.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}The mountains rose,
\par }{\QB the valleys sank down,
\par }{\QB to the place which you had assigned to them.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}You have set a boundary that they may not pass over,
\par }{\QB that they don’t turn again to cover the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}He sends springs into the valleys.
\par }{\QB They run among the mountains.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}They give drink to every animal of the field.
\par }{\QB The wild donkeys quench their thirst.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}The birds of the sky nest by them.
\par }{\QB They sing among the branches.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}He waters the mountains from his rooms.
\par }{\QB The earth is filled with the fruit of your works.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}He causes the grass to grow for the livestock,
\par }{\QB and plants for man to cultivate,
\par }{\QB that he may produce food out of the earth:
\par }{\Q \VS{15}wine that makes the heart of man glad,
\par }{\QB oil to make his face to shine,
\par }{\QB and bread that strengthens man’s heart.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Yahweh’s trees are well watered,
\par }{\QB the cedars of Lebanon, which he has planted;
\par }{\Q \VS{17}where the birds make their nests.
\par }{\QB The stork makes its home in the cypress trees.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}The high mountains are for the wild goats.
\par }{\QB The rocks are a refuge for the rock badgers.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}He appointed the moon for seasons.
\par }{\QB The sun knows when to set.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}You make darkness, and it is night,
\par }{\QB in which all the animals of the forest prowl.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}The young lions roar after their prey,
\par }{\QB and seek their food from God.
\par }{\Q \VS{22}The sun rises, and they steal away,
\par }{\QB and lie down in their dens.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Man goes out to his work,
\par }{\QB to his labor until the evening.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}Yahweh, how many are your works!
\par }{\QB In wisdom, you have made them all.
\par }{\QB The earth is full of your riches.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}There is the sea, great and wide,
\par }{\QB in which are innumerable living things,
\par }{\QB both small and large animals.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}There the ships go,
\par }{\QB and leviathan, whom you formed to play there.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}These all wait for you,
\par }{\QB that you may give them their food in due season.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}You give to them; they gather.
\par }{\QB You open your hand; they are satisfied with good.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}You hide your face; they are troubled.
\par }{\QB You take away their breath; they die and return to the dust.
\par }{\Q \VS{30}You send out your Spirit and they are created.
\par }{\QB You renew the face of the ground.
\par }{\Q \VS{31}Let Yahweh’s glory endure forever.
\par }{\QB Let Yahweh rejoice in his works.
\par }{\Q \VS{32}He looks at the earth, and it trembles.
\par }{\QB He touches the mountains, and they smoke.
\par }{\Q \VS{33}I will sing to Yahweh as long as I live.
\par }{\QB I will sing praise to my God while I have any being.
\par }{\Q \VS{34}Let my meditation be sweet to him.
\par }{\QB I will rejoice in Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{35}Let sinners be consumed out of the earth.
\par }{\QB Let the wicked be no more.
\par }{\QB Bless Yahweh, my soul.
\par }{\QB Praise Yah!

\par }\PsalmChap{105}{\Q \VerseOne{1}Give thanks to Yahweh! Call on his name!
\par }{\QB Make his doings known among the peoples.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Sing to him, sing praises to him!
\par }{\QB Tell of all his marvelous works.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Glory in his holy name.
\par }{\QB Let the heart of those who seek Yahweh rejoice.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Seek Yahweh and his strength.
\par }{\QB Seek his face forever more.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Remember his marvelous works that he has done:
\par }{\QB his wonders, and the judgments of his mouth,
\par }{\Q \VS{6}you offspring of Abraham, his servant,
\par }{\QB you children of Jacob, his chosen ones.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}He is Yahweh, our God.
\par }{\QB His judgments are in all the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}He has remembered his covenant forever,
\par }{\QB the word which he commanded to a thousand generations,
\par }{\Q \VS{9}the covenant which he made with Abraham,
\par }{\QB his oath to Isaac,
\par }{\Q \VS{10}and confirmed it to Jacob for a statute;
\par }{\QB to Israel for an everlasting covenant,
\par }{\Q \VS{11}saying, “To you I will give the land of Canaan,
\par }{\QB the lot of your inheritance,”
\par }{\Q \VS{12}when they were but a few men in number,
\par }{\QB yes, very few, and foreigners in it.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}They went about from nation to nation,
\par }{\QB from one kingdom to another people.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}He allowed no one to do them wrong.
\par }{\QB Yes, he reproved kings for their sakes,
\par }{\Q \VS{15}“Don’t touch my anointed ones!
\par }{\QB Do my prophets no harm!”
\par }{\Q \VS{16}He called for a famine on the land.
\par }{\QB He destroyed the food supplies.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}He sent a man before them.
\par }{\QB Joseph was sold for a slave.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}They bruised his feet with shackles.
\par }{\QB His neck was locked in irons,
\par }{\Q \VS{19}until the time that his word happened,
\par }{\QB and Yahweh’s word proved him true.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}The king sent and freed him,
\par }{\QB even the ruler of peoples, and let him go free.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}He made him lord of his house,
\par }{\QB and ruler of all of his possessions,
\par }{\Q \VS{22}to discipline his princes at his pleasure,
\par }{\QB and to teach his elders wisdom.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Israel also came into Egypt.
\par }{\QB Jacob lived in the land of Ham.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}He increased his people greatly,
\par }{\QB and made them stronger than their adversaries.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}He turned their heart to hate his people,
\par }{\QB to conspire against his servants.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}He sent Moses, his servant,
\par }{\QB and Aaron, whom he had chosen.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}They performed miracles among them,
\par }{\QB and wonders in the land of Ham.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}He sent darkness, and made it dark.
\par }{\QB They didn’t rebel against his words.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}He turned their waters into blood,
\par }{\QB and killed their fish.
\par }{\Q \VS{30}Their land swarmed with frogs,
\par }{\QB even in the rooms of their kings.
\par }{\Q \VS{31}He spoke, and swarms of flies came,
\par }{\QB and lice in all their borders.
\par }{\Q \VS{32}He gave them hail for rain,
\par }{\QB with lightning in their land.
\par }{\Q \VS{33}He struck their vines and also their fig trees,
\par }{\QB and shattered the trees of their country.
\par }{\Q \VS{34}He spoke, and the locusts came
\par }{\QB with the grasshoppers, without number,
\par }{\Q \VS{35}ate up every plant in their land,
\par }{\QB and ate up the fruit of their ground.
\par }{\Q \VS{36}He struck also all the firstborn in their land,
\par }{\QB the first fruits of all their manhood.
\par }{\Q \VS{37}He brought them out with silver and gold.
\par }{\QB There was not one feeble person among his tribes.
\par }{\Q \VS{38}Egypt was glad when they departed,
\par }{\QB for the fear of them had fallen on them.
\par }{\Q \VS{39}He spread a cloud for a covering,
\par }{\QB fire to give light in the night.
\par }{\Q \VS{40}They asked, and he brought quails,
\par }{\QB and satisfied them with the bread of the sky.
\par }{\Q \VS{41}He opened the rock, and waters gushed out.
\par }{\QB They ran as a river in the dry places.
\par }{\Q \VS{42}For he remembered his holy word,
\par }{\QB and Abraham, his servant.
\par }{\Q \VS{43}He brought his people out with joy,
\par }{\QB his chosen with singing.
\par }{\Q \VS{44}He gave them the lands of the nations.
\par }{\QB They took the labor of the peoples in possession,
\par }{\Q \VS{45}that they might keep his statutes,
\par }{\QB and observe his laws.
\par }{\QB Praise Yah!

\par }\PsalmChap{106}{\Q \VerseOne{1}Praise Yahweh!
\par }{\QB Give thanks to Yahweh, for he is good,
\par }{\QB for his loving kindness endures forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Who can utter the mighty acts of Yahweh,
\par }{\QB or fully declare all his praise?
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Blessed are those who keep justice.
\par }{\QB Blessed is one who does what is right at all times.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Remember me, Yahweh, with the favor that you show to your people.
\par }{\QB Visit me with your salvation,
\par }{\Q \VS{5}that I may see the prosperity of your chosen,
\par }{\QB that I may rejoice in the gladness of your nation,
\par }{\QB that I may glory with your inheritance.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{6}We have sinned with our fathers.
\par }{\QB We have committed iniquity.
\par }{\QB We have done wickedly.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Our fathers didn’t understand your wonders in Egypt.
\par }{\QB They didn’t remember the multitude of your loving kindnesses,
\par }{\QB but were rebellious at the sea, even at the Red Sea.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Nevertheless he saved them for his name’s sake,
\par }{\QB that he might make his mighty power known.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}He rebuked the Red Sea also, and it was dried up;
\par }{\QB so he led them through the depths, as through a desert.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}He saved them from the hand of him who hated them,
\par }{\QB and redeemed them from the hand of the enemy.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}The waters covered their adversaries.
\par }{\QB There was not one of them left.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Then they believed his words.
\par }{\QB They sang his praise.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{13}They soon forgot his works.
\par }{\QB They didn’t wait for his counsel,
\par }{\QB \VS{14}but gave in to craving in the desert,
\par }{\QB and tested God in the wasteland.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}He gave them their request,
\par }{\QB but sent leanness into their soul.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}They envied Moses also in the camp,
\par }{\QB and Aaron, Yahweh’s saint.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}The earth opened and swallowed up Dathan,
\par }{\QB and covered the company of Abiram.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}A fire was kindled in their company.
\par }{\QB The flame burned up the wicked.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}They made a calf in Horeb,
\par }{\QB and worshiped a molten image.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Thus they exchanged their glory
\par }{\QB for an image of a bull that eats grass.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}They forgot God, their Savior,
\par }{\QB who had done great things in Egypt,
\par }{\QB \VS{22}wondrous works in the land of Ham,
\par }{\QB and awesome things by the Red Sea.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Therefore he said that he would destroy them,
\par }{\QB had Moses, his chosen, not stood before him in the breach,
\par }{\QB to turn away his wrath, so that he wouldn’t destroy them.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}Yes, they despised the pleasant land.
\par }{\QB They didn’t believe his word,
\par }{\QB \VS{25}but murmured in their tents,
\par }{\QB and didn’t listen to Yahweh’s voice.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}Therefore he swore to them
\par }{\QB that he would overthrow them in the wilderness,
\par }{\QB \VS{27}that he would overthrow their offspring among the nations,
\par }{\QB and scatter them in the lands.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}They joined themselves also to Baal Peor,
\par }{\QB and ate the sacrifices of the dead.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}Thus they provoked him to anger with their deeds.
\par }{\QB The plague broke in on them.
\par }{\Q \VS{30}Then Phinehas stood up and executed judgment,
\par }{\QB so the plague was stopped.
\par }{\Q \VS{31}That was credited to him for righteousness,
\par }{\QB for all generations to come.
\par }{\Q \VS{32}They angered him also at the waters of Meribah,
\par }{\QB so that Moses was troubled for their sakes;
\par }{\Q \VS{33}because they were rebellious against his spirit,
\par }{\QB he spoke rashly with his lips.
\par }{\Q \VS{34}They didn’t destroy the peoples,
\par }{\QB as Yahweh commanded them,
\par }{\QB \VS{35}but mixed themselves with the nations,
\par }{\QB and learned their works.
\par }{\Q \VS{36}They served their idols,
\par }{\QB which became a snare to them.
\par }{\Q \VS{37}Yes, they sacrificed their sons and their daughters to demons.
\par }{\QB \VS{38}They shed innocent blood,
\par }{\QB even the blood of their sons and of their daughters,
\par }{\QB whom they sacrificed to the idols of Canaan.
\par }{\QB The land was polluted with blood.
\par }{\Q \VS{39}Thus they were defiled with their works,
\par }{\QB and prostituted themselves in their deeds.
\par }{\Q \VS{40}Therefore Yahweh burned with anger against his people.
\par }{\QB He abhorred his inheritance.
\par }{\Q \VS{41}He gave them into the hand of the nations.
\par }{\QB Those who hated them ruled over them.
\par }{\Q \VS{42}Their enemies also oppressed them.
\par }{\QB They were brought into subjection under their hand.
\par }{\Q \VS{43}He rescued them many times,
\par }{\QB but they were rebellious in their counsel,
\par }{\QB and were brought low in their iniquity.
\par }{\Q \VS{44}Nevertheless he regarded their distress,
\par }{\QB when he heard their cry.
\par }{\Q \VS{45}He remembered for them his covenant,
\par }{\QB and repented according to the multitude of his loving kindnesses.
\par }{\Q \VS{46}He made them also to be pitied
\par }{\QB by all those who carried them captive.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{47}Save us, Yahweh, our God,
\par }{\QB gather us from among the nations,
\par }{\QB to give thanks to your holy name,
\par }{\QB to triumph in your praise!
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{48}Blessed be Yahweh, the God of Israel,
\par }{\QB from everlasting even to everlasting!
\par }{\Q Let all the people say, “Amen.”
\par }{\Q Praise Yah!

\par }\PsalmChap{107}{\Q \VerseOne{1}Give thanks to Yahweh,\FTNT{*}{{\FR 107:1 }
“Yahweh” is God’s proper Name, sometimes rendered “LORD” (all caps) in other translations.} for he is good,
\par }{\QB for his loving kindness endures forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Let the redeemed by Yahweh say so,
\par }{\QB whom he has redeemed from the hand of the adversary,
\par }{\QB \VS{3}And gathered out of the lands,
\par }{\QB from the east and from the west,
\par }{\QB from the north and from the south.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{4}They wandered in the wilderness in a desert way.
\par }{\QB They found no city to live in.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Hungry and thirsty,
\par }{\QB their soul fainted in them.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Then they cried to Yahweh in their trouble,
\par }{\QB and he delivered them out of their distresses,
\par }{\Q \VS{7}he led them also by a straight way,
\par }{\QB that they might go to a city to live in.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Let them praise Yahweh for his loving kindness,
\par }{\QB for his wonderful deeds to the children of men!
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{9}For he satisfies the longing soul.
\par }{\QB He fills the hungry soul with good.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{10}Some sat in darkness and in the shadow of death,
\par }{\QB being bound in affliction and iron,
\par }{\QB \VS{11}because they rebelled against the words of God,\FTNT{†}{{\FR 107:11 }
The Hebrew word rendered “God” is “אֱלֹהִ֑ים” (Elohim).}
\par }{\QB and condemned the counsel of the Most High.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Therefore he brought down their heart with labor.
\par }{\QB They fell down, and there was no one to help.

\par }{\QB and he saved them out of their distresses.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}He brought them out of darkness and the shadow of death,

\par }{\QB for his wonderful deeds to the children of men!
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{16}For he has broken the gates of bronze,
\par }{\QB and cut through bars of iron.

\par }{\QB and because of their iniquities.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Their soul abhors all kinds of food.
\par }{\QB They draw near to the gates of death.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Then they cry to Yahweh in their trouble,
\par }{\QB he saves them out of their distresses.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}He sends his word, and heals them,
\par }{\QB and delivers them from their graves.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Let them praise Yahweh for his loving kindness,
\par }{\QB for his wonderful deeds to the children of men!
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{22}Let them offer the sacrifices of thanksgiving,
\par }{\QB and declare his deeds with singing.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{23}Those who go down to the sea in ships,
\par }{\QB who do business in great waters;
\par }{\QB \VS{24}These see Yahweh’s deeds,
\par }{\QB and his wonders in the deep.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}For he commands, and raises the stormy wind,
\par }{\QB which lifts up its waves.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}They mount up to the sky; they go down again to the depths.
\par }{\QB Their soul melts away because of trouble.
\par }{\Q \VS{27}They reel back and forth, and stagger like a drunken man,
\par }{\QB and are at their wits’ end.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}Then they cry to Yahweh in their trouble,
\par }{\QB and he brings them out of their distress.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}He makes the storm a calm,
\par }{\QB so that its waves are still.
\par }{\Q \VS{30}Then they are glad because it is calm,
\par }{\QB so he brings them to their desired haven.
\par }{\Q \VS{31}Let them praise Yahweh for his loving kindness,
\par }{\QB for his wonderful deeds for the children of men!
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{32}Let them exalt him also in the assembly of the people,
\par }{\QB and praise him in the seat of the elders.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{33}He turns rivers into a desert,
\par }{\QB water springs into a thirsty ground,
\par }{\QB \VS{34}and a fruitful land into a salt waste,
\par }{\QB for the wickedness of those who dwell in it.
\par }{\Q \VS{35}He turns a desert into a pool of water,
\par }{\QB and a dry land into water springs.
\par }{\Q \VS{36}There he makes the hungry live,
\par }{\QB that they may prepare a city to live in,
\par }{\QB \VS{37}sow fields, plant vineyards,
\par }{\QB and reap the fruits of increase.
\par }{\Q \VS{38}He blesses them also, so that they are multiplied greatly.
\par }{\QB He doesn’t allow their livestock to decrease.
\par }{\Q \VS{39}Again, they are diminished and bowed down
\par }{\QB through oppression, trouble, and sorrow.
\par }{\Q \VS{40}He pours contempt on princes,
\par }{\QB and causes them to wander in a trackless waste.
\par }{\Q \VS{41}Yet he lifts the needy out of their affliction,
\par }{\QB and increases their families like a flock.
\par }{\Q \VS{42}The upright will see it, and be glad.
\par }{\QB All the wicked will shut their mouths.
\par }{\Q \VS{43}Whoever is wise will pay attention to these things.
\par }{\QB They will consider the loving kindnesses of Yahweh.

\par }\PsalmChap{108}{\D A Song. A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}My heart is steadfast, God.
\par }{\QB I will sing and I will make music with my soul.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Wake up, harp and lyre!
\par }{\QB I will wake up the dawn.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}I will give thanks to you, Yahweh, among the nations.
\par }{\QB I will sing praises to you among the peoples.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For your loving kindness is great above the heavens.
\par }{\QB Your faithfulness reaches to the skies.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Be exalted, God, above the heavens!
\par }{\QB Let your glory be over all the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}That your beloved may be delivered,
\par }{\QB save with your right hand, and answer us.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}God has spoken from his sanctuary: “In triumph,
\par }{\QB I will divide Shechem, and measure out the valley of Succoth.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Gilead is mine. Manasseh is mine.
\par }{\QB Ephraim also is my helmet.
\par }{\QB Judah is my scepter.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Moab is my wash pot.
\par }{\QB I will toss my sandal on Edom.
\par }{\QB I will shout over Philistia.”
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Who will bring me into the fortified city?
\par }{\QB Who has led me to Edom?
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Haven’t you rejected us, God?
\par }{\QB You don’t go out, God, with our armies.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Give us help against the enemy,
\par }{\QB for the help of man is vain.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Through God, we will do valiantly.
\par }{\QB For it is he who will tread down our enemies.

\par }\PsalmChap{109}{\D For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}God of my praise, don’t remain silent,
\par }{\QB \VS{2}for they have opened the mouth of the wicked and the mouth of deceit against me.
\par }{\QB They have spoken to me with a lying tongue.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}They have also surrounded me with words of hatred,
\par }{\QB and fought against me without a cause.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}In return for my love, they are my adversaries;
\par }{\QB but I am in prayer.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}They have rewarded me evil for good,
\par }{\QB and hatred for my love.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Set a wicked man over him.
\par }{\QB Let an adversary stand at his right hand.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}When he is judged, let him come out guilty.
\par }{\QB Let his prayer be turned into sin.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Let his days be few.
\par }{\QB Let another take his office.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Let his children be fatherless,
\par }{\QB and his wife a widow.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Let his children be wandering beggars.
\par }{\QB Let them be sought from their ruins.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Let the creditor seize all that he has.
\par }{\QB Let strangers plunder the fruit of his labor.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Let there be no one to extend kindness to him,
\par }{\QB neither let there be anyone to have pity on his fatherless children.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Let his posterity be cut off.
\par }{\QB In the generation following let their name be blotted out.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Let the iniquity of his fathers be remembered by Yahweh.
\par }{\QB Don’t let the sin of his mother be blotted out.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}Let them be before Yahweh continually,
\par }{\QB that he may cut off their memory from the earth;
\par }{\Q \VS{16}because he didn’t remember to show kindness,
\par }{\QB but persecuted the poor and needy man,
\par }{\QB the broken in heart, to kill them.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Yes, he loved cursing, and it came to him.
\par }{\QB He didn’t delight in blessing, and it was far from him.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}He clothed himself also with cursing as with his garment.
\par }{\QB It came into his inward parts like water,
\par }{\QB like oil into his bones.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}Let it be to him as the clothing with which he covers himself,
\par }{\QB for the belt that is always around him.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}This is the reward of my adversaries from Yahweh,
\par }{\QB of those who speak evil against my soul.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{21}But deal with me, Yahweh the Lord,\FTNT{*}{{\FR 109:21 }
The word translated “Lord” is “Adonai.”} for your name’s sake,
\par }{\QB because your loving kindness is good, deliver me;
\par }{\QB \VS{22}for I am poor and needy.
\par }{\QB My heart is wounded within me.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}I fade away like an evening shadow.
\par }{\QB I am shaken off like a locust.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}My knees are weak through fasting.
\par }{\QB My body is thin and lacks fat.
\par }{\Q \VS{25}I have also become a reproach to them.
\par }{\QB When they see me, they shake their head.
\par }{\Q \VS{26}Help me, Yahweh, my God.
\par }{\QB Save me according to your loving kindness;
\par }{\Q \VS{27}that they may know that this is your hand;
\par }{\QB that you, Yahweh, have done it.
\par }{\Q \VS{28}They may curse, but you bless.
\par }{\QB When they arise, they will be shamed,
\par }{\QB but your servant shall rejoice.
\par }{\Q \VS{29}Let my adversaries be clothed with dishonor.
\par }{\QB Let them cover themselves with their own shame as with a robe.
\par }{\Q \VS{30}I will give great thanks to Yahweh with my mouth.
\par }{\QB Yes, I will praise him among the multitude.
\par }{\Q \VS{31}For he will stand at the right hand of the needy,
\par }{\QB to save him from those who judge his soul.

\par }{\QB “You are a priest forever in the order of Melchizedek.”
\par }{\Q \VS{5}The Lord is at your right hand.

\par }{\QB He will crush the ruler of the whole earth.

\par }{\QB therefore he will lift up his head.

\par }{\QB All those who do his work have a good understanding.

\par }{\Q \VS{75}Yahweh, I know that your judgments are righteous,
\par }{\QB that in faithfulness you have afflicted me.
\par }{\Q \VS{76}Please let your loving kindness be for my comfort,
\par }{\QB according to your word to your servant.
\par }{\Q \VS{77}Let your tender mercies come to me, that I may live;
\par }{\QB for your law is my delight.
\par }{\Q \VS{78}Let the proud be disappointed, for they have overthrown me wrongfully.
\par }{\QB I will meditate on your precepts.
\par }{\Q \VS{79}Let those who fear you turn to me.
\par }{\QB They will know your statutes.
\par }{\Q \VS{80}Let my heart be blameless toward your decrees,
\par }{\QB that I may not be disappointed.
\par }{\D KAF
\par }{\Q \VS{81}My soul faints for your salvation.
\par }{\QB I hope in your word.
\par }{\Q \VS{82}My eyes fail for your word.
\par }{\QB I say, “When will you comfort me?”
\par }{\Q \VS{83}For I have become like a wineskin in the smoke.
\par }{\QB I don’t forget your statutes.
\par }{\Q \VS{84}How many are the days of your servant?
\par }{\QB When will you execute judgment on those who persecute me?
\par }{\Q \VS{85}The proud have dug pits for me,
\par }{\QB contrary to your law.
\par }{\Q \VS{86}All of your commandments are faithful.
\par }{\QB They persecute me wrongfully.
\par }{\QB Help me!
\par }{\Q \VS{87}They had almost wiped me from the earth,
\par }{\QB but I didn’t forsake your precepts.
\par }{\Q \VS{88}Preserve my life according to your loving kindness,
\par }{\QB so I will obey the statutes of your mouth.
\par }{\D LAMED
\par }{\Q \VS{89}Yahweh, your word is settled in heaven forever.
\par }{\Q \VS{90}Your faithfulness is to all generations.
\par }{\QB You have established the earth, and it remains.
\par }{\Q \VS{91}Your laws remain to this day,
\par }{\QB for all things serve you.
\par }{\Q \VS{92}Unless your law had been my delight,
\par }{\QB I would have perished in my affliction.
\par }{\Q \VS{93}I will never forget your precepts,
\par }{\QB for with them, you have revived me.
\par }{\Q \VS{94}I am yours.
\par }{\QB Save me, for I have sought your precepts.
\par }{\Q \VS{95}The wicked have waited for me, to destroy me.
\par }{\QB I will consider your statutes.
\par }{\Q \VS{96}I have seen a limit to all perfection,
\par }{\QB but your commands are boundless.
\par }{\D MEM
\par }{\Q \VS{97}How I love your law!
\par }{\QB It is my meditation all day.
\par }{\Q \VS{98}Your commandments make me wiser than my enemies,
\par }{\QB for your commandments are always with me.
\par }{\Q \VS{99}I have more understanding than all my teachers,
\par }{\QB for your testimonies are my meditation.
\par }{\Q \VS{100}I understand more than the aged,
\par }{\QB because I have kept your precepts.
\par }{\Q \VS{101}I have kept my feet from every evil way,
\par }{\QB that I might observe your word.
\par }{\Q \VS{102}I have not turned away from your ordinances,
\par }{\QB for you have taught me.
\par }{\Q \VS{103}How sweet are your promises to my taste,
\par }{\QB more than honey to my mouth!
\par }{\Q \VS{104}Through your precepts, I get understanding;
\par }{\QB therefore I hate every false way.

\par }{\QB Praise Yahweh’s name!
\par }{\QB Praise him, you servants of Yahweh,
\par }{\Q \VS{2}you who stand in Yahweh’s house,
\par }{\QB in the courts of our God’s house.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Praise Yah, for Yahweh is good.
\par }{\QB Sing praises to his name, for that is pleasant.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For Yah has chosen Jacob for himself,
\par }{\QB Israel for his own possession.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}For I know that Yahweh is great,
\par }{\QB that our Lord is above all gods.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Whatever Yahweh pleased, that he has done,
\par }{\QB in heaven and in earth, in the seas and in all deeps.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}He causes the clouds to rise from the ends of the earth.
\par }{\QB He makes lightnings with the rain.
\par }{\QB He brings the wind out of his treasuries.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}He struck the firstborn of Egypt,
\par }{\QB both of man and animal.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}He sent signs and wonders into the middle of you, Egypt,
\par }{\QB on Pharaoh, and on all his servants.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}He struck many nations,
\par }{\QB and killed mighty kings,
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Sihon king of the Amorites,
\par }{\QB Og king of Bashan,
\par }{\QB and all the kingdoms of Canaan,
\par }{\Q \VS{12}and gave their land for a heritage,
\par }{\QB a heritage to Israel, his people.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Your name, Yahweh, endures forever;
\par }{\QB your renown, Yahweh, throughout all generations.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}For Yahweh will judge his people
\par }{\QB and have compassion on his servants.
\par }{\BB \par }{\Q \VS{15}The idols of the nations are silver and gold,
\par }{\QB the work of men’s hands.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}They have mouths, but they can’t speak.
\par }{\QB They have eyes, but they can’t see.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}They have ears, but they can’t hear,
\par }{\QB neither is there any breath in their mouths.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Those who make them will be like them,
\par }{\QB yes, everyone who trusts in them.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}House of Israel, praise Yahweh!
\par }{\QB House of Aaron, praise Yahweh!
\par }{\Q \VS{20}House of Levi, praise Yahweh!
\par }{\QB You who fear Yahweh, praise Yahweh!
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Blessed be Yahweh from Zion,
\par }{\QB who dwells at Jerusalem.
\par }{\Q Praise Yah!

\par }\PsalmChap{136}{\Q \VerseOne{1}Give thanks to Yahweh, for he is good;
