\par }\PsalmChap{138}{\D By David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}I will give you thanks with my whole heart.
\par }{\QB Before the gods,\FTNT{*}{{\FR 138:1 }
The word elohim, used here, usually means “God” but can also mean “gods”, “princes”, or “angels”.} I will sing praises to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}I will bow down toward your holy temple,
\par }{\QB and give thanks to your Name for your loving kindness and for your truth;
\par }{\QB for you have exalted your Name and your Word above all.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}In the day that I called, you answered me.
\par }{\QB You encouraged me with strength in my soul.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}All the kings of the earth will give you thanks, Yahweh,
\par }{\QB for they have heard the words of your mouth.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Yes, they will sing of the ways of Yahweh,
\par }{\QB for Yahweh’s glory is great!
\par }{\Q \VS{6}For though Yahweh is high, yet he looks after the lowly;
\par }{\QB but he knows the proud from afar.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Though I walk in the middle of trouble, you will revive me.
\par }{\QB You will stretch out your hand against the wrath of my enemies.
\par }{\QB Your right hand will save me.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Yahweh will fulfill that which concerns me.
\par }{\QB Your loving kindness, Yahweh, endures forever.
\par }{\QB Don’t forsake the works of your own hands.

\par }\PsalmChap{139}{\D For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Yahweh, you have searched me,
\par }{\QB and you know me.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}You know my sitting down and my rising up.
\par }{\QB You perceive my thoughts from afar.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}You search out my path and my lying down,
\par }{\QB and are acquainted with all my ways.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For there is not a word on my tongue,
\par }{\QB but, behold, Yahweh, you know it altogether.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}You hem me in behind and before.
\par }{\QB You laid your hand on me.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}This knowledge is beyond me.
\par }{\QB It’s lofty.
\par }{\QB I can’t attain it.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Where could I go from your Spirit?
\par }{\QB Or where could I flee from your presence?
\par }{\Q \VS{8}If I ascend up into heaven, you are there.
\par }{\QB If I make my bed in Sheol,\FTNT{*}{{\FR 139:8 }
Sheol is the place of the dead.} behold, you are there!
\par }{\Q \VS{9}If I take the wings of the dawn,
\par }{\QB and settle in the uttermost parts of the sea,
\par }{\Q \VS{10}even there your hand will lead me,
\par }{\QB and your right hand will hold me.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}If I say, “Surely the darkness will overwhelm me.
\par }{\QB The light around me will be night,”
\par }{\Q \VS{12}even the darkness doesn’t hide from you,
\par }{\QB but the night shines as the day.
\par }{\QB The darkness is like light to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}For you formed my inmost being.
\par }{\QB You knit me together in my mother’s womb.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}I will give thanks to you,
\par }{\QB for I am fearfully and wonderfully made.
\par }{\Q Your works are wonderful.
\par }{\QB My soul knows that very well.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}My frame wasn’t hidden from you,
\par }{\QB when I was made in secret,
\par }{\QB woven together in the depths of the earth.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}Your eyes saw my body.
\par }{\QB In your book they were all written,
\par }{\QB the days that were ordained for me,
\par }{\QB when as yet there were none of them.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}How precious to me are your thoughts, God!
\par }{\QB How vast is their sum!
\par }{\Q \VS{18}If I would count them, they are more in number than the sand.
\par }{\QB When I wake up, I am still with you.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}If only you, God, would kill the wicked.
\par }{\QB Get away from me, you bloodthirsty men!
\par }{\Q \VS{20}For they speak against you wickedly.
\par }{\QB Your enemies take your name in vain.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}Yahweh, don’t I hate those who hate you?
\par }{\QB Am I not grieved with those who rise up against you?
\par }{\Q \VS{22}I hate them with perfect hatred.
\par }{\QB They have become my enemies.
\par }{\Q \VS{23}Search me, God, and know my heart.
\par }{\QB Try me, and know my thoughts.
\par }{\Q \VS{24}See if there is any wicked way in me,
\par }{\QB and lead me in the everlasting way.

\par }\PsalmChap{140}{\D For the Chief Musician. A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Deliver me, Yahweh, from the evil man.
\par }{\QB Preserve me from the violent man:
\par }{\Q \VS{2}those who devise mischief in their hearts.
\par }{\QB They continually gather themselves together for war.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}They have sharpened their tongues like a serpent.
\par }{\QB Viper’s poison is under their lips.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{4}Yahweh, keep me from the hands of the wicked.
\par }{\QB Preserve me from the violent men who have determined to trip my feet.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}The proud have hidden a snare for me,
\par }{\QB they have spread the cords of a net by the path.
\par }{\QB They have set traps for me.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{6}I said to Yahweh, “You are my God.”
\par }{\QB Listen to the cry of my petitions, Yahweh.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Yahweh, the Lord, the strength of my salvation,
\par }{\QB you have covered my head in the day of battle.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Yahweh, don’t grant the desires of the wicked.
\par }{\QB Don’t let their evil plans succeed, or they will become proud.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{9}As for the head of those who surround me,
\par }{\QB let the mischief of their own lips cover them.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Let burning coals fall on them.
\par }{\QB Let them be thrown into the fire,
\par }{\QB into miry pits, from where they never rise.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}An evil speaker won’t be established in the earth.
\par }{\QB Evil will hunt the violent man to overthrow him.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}I know that Yahweh will maintain the cause of the afflicted,
\par }{\QB and justice for the needy.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Surely the righteous will give thanks to your name.
\par }{\QB The upright will dwell in your presence.

\par }\PsalmChap{141}{\D A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Yahweh, I have called on you.
\par }{\QB Come to me quickly!
\par }{\QB Listen to my voice when I call to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Let my prayer be set before you like incense;
\par }{\QB the lifting up of my hands like the evening sacrifice.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Set a watch, Yahweh, before my mouth.
\par }{\QB Keep the door of my lips.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Don’t incline my heart to any evil thing,
\par }{\QB to practice deeds of wickedness with men who work iniquity.
\par }{\QB Don’t let me eat of their delicacies.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Let the righteous strike me, it is kindness;
\par }{\QB let him reprove me, it is like oil on the head;
\par }{\QB don’t let my head refuse it;
\par }{\QB Yet my prayer is always against evil deeds.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Their judges are thrown down by the sides of the rock.
\par }{\QB They will hear my words, for they are well spoken.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}“As when one plows and breaks up the earth,
\par }{\QB our bones are scattered at the mouth of Sheol.”\FTNT{*}{{\FR 141:7 }
Sheol is the place of the dead.}
\par }{\Q \VS{8}For my eyes are on you, Yahweh, the Lord.
\par }{\QB In you, I take refuge.
\par }{\QB Don’t leave my soul destitute.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Keep me from the snare which they have laid for me,
\par }{\QB from the traps of the workers of iniquity.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Let the wicked fall together into their own nets
\par }{\QB while I pass by.

\par }{\QB for there is no one who is concerned for me.

\par }{\QB No one cares for my soul.

\par }{\QB I said, “You are my refuge,
\par }{\QB my portion in the land of the living.”

\par }{\QB for I am in desperate need.

\par }{\Q \VS{7}Bring my soul out of prison,
\par }{\QB that I may give thanks to your name.
\par }{\Q The righteous will surround me,
\par }{\QB for you will be good to me.

\par }\PsalmChap{143}{\D A Psalm by David.
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}Hear my prayer, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB Listen to my petitions.
\par }{\QB In your faithfulness and righteousness, relieve me.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Don’t enter into judgment with your servant,
\par }{\QB for in your sight no man living is righteous.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}For the enemy pursues my soul.
\par }{\QB He has struck my life down to the ground.
\par }{\QB He has made me live in dark places, as those who have been long dead.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Therefore my spirit is overwhelmed within me.
\par }{\QB My heart within me is desolate.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}I remember the days of old.
\par }{\QB I meditate on all your doings.
\par }{\QB I contemplate the work of your hands.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}I spread out my hands to you.
\par }{\QB My soul thirsts for you, like a parched land.
\par }{\QS Selah.\par }
{\Q \VS{7}Hurry to answer me, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB My spirit fails.
\par }{\Q Don’t hide your face from me,
\par }{\QB so that I don’t become like those who go down into the pit.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Cause me to hear your loving kindness in the morning,
\par }{\QB for I trust in you.
\par }{\Q Cause me to know the way in which I should walk,
\par }{\QB for I lift up my soul to you.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Deliver me, Yahweh, from my enemies.
\par }{\QB I flee to you to hide me.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}Teach me to do your will,
\par }{\QB for you are my God.
\par }{\Q Your Spirit is good.
\par }{\QB Lead me in the land of uprightness.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Revive me, Yahweh, for your name’s sake.
\par }{\QB In your righteousness, bring my soul out of trouble.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}In your loving kindness, cut off my enemies,
\par }{\QB and destroy all those who afflict my soul,
\par }{\QB For I am your servant.

\par }{\QB whose right hand is a right hand of falsehood.

\par }{\QB who rescues David, his servant, from the deadly sword.

\par }{\QB whose right hand is a right hand of falsehood.

\par }\PsalmChap{145}{\D A praise psalm by David.\FTNT{*}{{\FR 145: }
This is an acrostic psalm, with every verse (including the second half of verse 13) starting with a consecutive letter of the Hebrew alphabet.}
\par }{\Q \VerseOne{1}I will exalt you, my God, the King.
\par }{\QB I will praise your name forever and ever.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Every day I will praise you.
\par }{\QB I will extol your name forever and ever.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Great is Yahweh, and greatly to be praised!
\par }{\QB His greatness is unsearchable.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}One generation will commend your works to another,
\par }{\QB and will declare your mighty acts.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}I will meditate on the glorious majesty of your honor,
\par }{\QB on your wondrous works.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Men will speak of the might of your awesome acts.
\par }{\QB I will declare your greatness.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}They will utter the memory of your great goodness,
\par }{\QB and will sing of your righteousness.
\par }{\Q \VS{8}Yahweh is gracious, merciful,
\par }{\QB slow to anger, and of great loving kindness.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}Yahweh is good to all.
\par }{\QB His tender mercies are over all his works.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}All your works will give thanks to you, Yahweh.
\par }{\QB Your saints will extol you.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}They will speak of the glory of your kingdom,
\par }{\QB and talk about your power,
\par }{\Q \VS{12}to make known to the sons of men his mighty acts,
\par }{\QB the glory of the majesty of his kingdom.
\par }{\Q \VS{13}Your kingdom is an everlasting kingdom.
\par }{\QB Your dominion endures throughout all generations.
\par }{\Q Yahweh is faithful in all his words,
\par }{\QB and loving in all his deeds.\FTNT{†}{{\FR 145:13 }
Some manuscripts omit these last two lines.}
\par }{\Q \VS{14}Yahweh upholds all who fall,
\par }{\QB and raises up all those who are bowed down.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}The eyes of all wait for you.
\par }{\QB You give them their food in due season.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}You open your hand,
\par }{\QB and satisfy the desire of every living thing.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}Yahweh is righteous in all his ways,
\par }{\QB and gracious in all his works.
\par }{\Q \VS{18}Yahweh is near to all those who call on him,
\par }{\QB to all who call on him in truth.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}He will fulfill the desire of those who fear him.
\par }{\QB He also will hear their cry, and will save them.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}Yahweh preserves all those who love him,
\par }{\QB but he will destroy all the wicked.
\par }{\Q \VS{21}My mouth will speak the praise of Yahweh.
\par }{\QB Let all flesh bless his holy name forever and ever.
\par }{\BB \par }

\PsalmChap{147}{\Q \VerseOne{1}Praise Yah,
\par }{\QB for it is good to sing praises to our God;
\par }{\QB for it is pleasant and fitting to praise him.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Yahweh builds up Jerusalem.
\par }{\QB He gathers together the outcasts of Israel.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}He heals the broken in heart,
\par }{\QB and binds up their wounds.
\par }{\Q \VS{4}He counts the number of the stars.
\par }{\QB He calls them all by their names.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Great is our Lord, and mighty in power.
\par }{\QB His understanding is infinite.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Yahweh upholds the humble.
\par }{\QB He brings the wicked down to the ground.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Sing to Yahweh with thanksgiving.
\par }{\QB Sing praises on the harp to our God,
\par }{\Q \VS{8}who covers the sky with clouds,
\par }{\QB who prepares rain for the earth,
\par }{\QB who makes grass grow on the mountains.
\par }{\Q \VS{9}He provides food for the livestock,
\par }{\QB and for the young ravens when they call.
\par }{\Q \VS{10}He doesn’t delight in the strength of the horse.
\par }{\QB He takes no pleasure in the legs of a man.
\par }{\Q \VS{11}Yahweh takes pleasure in those who fear him,
\par }{\QB in those who hope in his loving kindness.
\par }{\Q \VS{12}Praise Yahweh, Jerusalem!
\par }{\QB Praise your God, Zion!
\par }{\Q \VS{13}For he has strengthened the bars of your gates.
\par }{\QB He has blessed your children within you.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}He makes peace in your borders.
\par }{\QB He fills you with the finest of the wheat.
\par }{\Q \VS{15}He sends out his commandment to the earth.
\par }{\QB His word runs very swiftly.
\par }{\Q \VS{16}He gives snow like wool,
\par }{\QB and scatters frost like ashes.
\par }{\Q \VS{17}He hurls down his hail like pebbles.
\par }{\QB Who can stand before his cold?
\par }{\Q \VS{18}He sends out his word, and melts them.
\par }{\QB He causes his wind to blow, and the waters flow.
\par }{\Q \VS{19}He shows his word to Jacob,
\par }{\QB his statutes and his ordinances to Israel.
\par }{\Q \VS{20}He has not done this for just any nation.
\par }{\QB They don’t know his ordinances.
\par }{\Q Praise Yah!
\par }{\BB \par }
\PsalmChap{148}{\Q \VerseOne{1}Praise Yah!
\par }{\QB Praise Yahweh from the heavens!
\par }{\QB Praise him in the heights!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Praise him, all his angels!
\par }{\QB Praise him, all his army!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Praise him, sun and moon!
\par }{\QB Praise him, all you shining stars!
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Praise him, you heavens of heavens,
\par }{\QB you waters that are above the heavens.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Let them praise Yahweh’s name,
\par }{\QB for he commanded, and they were created.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}He has also established them forever and ever.
\par }{\QB He has made a decree which will not pass away.
\par }{\Q \VS{7}Praise Yahweh from the earth,
\par }{\QB you great sea creatures, and all depths;
\par }{\Q \VS{8}lightning and hail, snow and clouds;
\par }{\QB stormy wind, fulfilling his word;
\par }{\Q \VS{9}mountains and all hills;
\par }{\QB fruit trees and all cedars;
\par }{\Q \VS{10}wild animals and all livestock;
\par }{\QB small creatures and flying birds;
\par }{\Q \VS{11}kings of the earth and all peoples;
\par }{\QB princes and all judges of the earth;
\par }{\Q \VS{12}both young men and maidens;
\par }{\QB old men and children:
\par }{\Q \VS{13}let them praise Yahweh’s name,
\par }{\QB for his name alone is exalted.
\par }{\QB His glory is above the earth and the heavens.
\par }{\Q \VS{14}He has lifted up the horn of his people,
\par }{\QB the praise of all his saints,
\par }{\QB even of the children of Israel, a people near to him.
\par }{\Q Praise Yah!
\par }{\BB \par }
\PsalmChap{149}{\Q \VerseOne{1}Praise Yahweh!
\par }{\QB Sing to Yahweh a new song,
\par }{\QB his praise in the assembly of the saints.
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Let Israel rejoice in him who made them.
\par }{\QB Let the children of Zion be joyful in their King.
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Let them praise his name in the dance!
\par }{\QB Let them sing praises to him with tambourine and harp!
\par }{\Q \VS{4}For Yahweh takes pleasure in his people.
\par }{\QB He crowns the humble with salvation.
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Let the saints rejoice in honor.
\par }{\QB Let them sing for joy on their beds.
\par }{\Q \VS{6}May the high praises of God be in their mouths,
\par }{\QB and a two-edged sword in their hand,
\par }{\Q \VS{7}to execute vengeance on the nations,
\par }{\QB and punishments on the peoples;
\par }{\Q \VS{8}to bind their kings with chains,
\par }{\QB and their nobles with fetters of iron;
\par }{\Q \VS{9}to execute on them the written judgment.
\par }{\QB All his saints have this honor.
\par }{\Q Praise Yah!
\par }{\BB \par }
\PsalmChap{150}{\Q \VerseOne{1}Praise Yah!
\par }{\QB Praise God in his sanctuary!
\par }{\QB Praise him in his heavens for his acts of power!
\par }{\Q \VS{2}Praise him for his mighty acts!
\par }{\QB Praise him according to his excellent greatness!
\par }{\Q \VS{3}Praise him with the sounding of the trumpet!
\par }{\QB Praise him with harp and lyre!
\par }{\Q \VS{4}Praise him with tambourine and dancing!
\par }{\QB Praise him with stringed instruments and flute!
\par }{\Q \VS{5}Praise him with loud cymbals!
\par }{\QB Praise him with resounding cymbals!
\par }{\Q \VS{6}Let everything that has breath praise Yah!
\par }{\QB Praise Yah!
\par }
